931:             authorId: resolveId(log.authorId, idMap) ?? userId,
932:             logType: log.logType,
933:             contentText: log.contentText ?? "",
934:             contentMeta: j(log.contentMeta),
935:           },
936:         });
937:         idMap.set(log.id, created.id);
938:       }
939: 
940:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
941:       // 8. AppNotification（仅追加新建的；已有的仅更新 readAt）
942:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
943:       for (const notif of snap.notifications ?? []) {
944:         if (isTempId(notif.id)) {
945:           const created = await tx.appNotification.create({
946:             data: {
947:               recipientId: resolveId(notif.recipientId, idMap) ?? userId,
948:               actorId: notif.actorId ? resolveId(notif.actorId, idMap) : null,
949:               kind: notif.kind,
950:               title: notif.title,
951:               body: notif.body ?? null,
952:               refNodeId: notif.refNodeId ? resolveId(notif.refNodeId, idMap) : null,
953:               refAssignmentId: notif.refAssignmentId
954:                 ? resolveId(notif.refAssignmentId, idMap)
955:                 : null,
956:               refFollowGrantId: notif.refFollowGrantId
957:                 ? resolveId(notif.refFollowGrantId, idMap)
958:                 : null,
959:               refReportId: notif.refReportId
960:                 ? resolveId(notif.refReportId, idMap)
961:                 : null,
962:               readAt: notif.readAt ? new Date(notif.readAt) : null,
963:               calendarProvider: notif.calendarProvider ?? null,
964:             },
965:           });
966:           idMap.set(notif.id, created.id);
967:         } else {
968:           const dbId = parseDbId(notif.id);
969:           if (!dbId) continue;
970:           await tx.appNotification.updateMany({
971:             where: { id: dbId, recipientId: userId },
972:             data: { readAt: notif.readAt ? new Date(notif.readAt) : null },
973:           });
974:         }
975:       }
976: 
977:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
978:       // 9. Relationship（联系线）
979:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
980:       const snapRelIds = new Set<number>();
981:       for (const rel of snap.relationships ?? []) {
982:         if (isTempId(rel.id)) {
983:           const mindmapDbId = resolveId(rel.mindmapId, idMap);
984:           const fromDbId = resolveId(rel.fromId, idMap);
985:           const toDbId = resolveId(rel.toId, idMap);
986:           if (!mindmapDbId || !fromDbId || !toDbId) continue;
987:           const created = await tx.relationship.create({
988:             data: {
989:               mindmapId: mindmapDbId,
990:               fromId: fromDbId,
991:               toId: toDbId,
992:               label: rel.label ?? null,
993:               createdBy: userId,
994:             },
995:           });
996:           idMap.set(rel.id, created.id);
997:           snapRelIds.add(created.id);
998:         } else {
999:           const dbId = parseDbId(rel.id);
1000:           if (!dbId) continue;
1001:           snapRelIds.add(dbId);
1002:         }
1003:       }
1004:       // 删除快照中不存在的联系线
1005:       // 规范 4-2：Relationship 无 mindmap 关联模型，用 createdBy: userId 限定
1006:       // 只删当前用户创建的联系线，防止误删下属导图的联系线（下属导图 ID 会
1007:       // 出现在 snapMindmapIds 中，但其联系线的 createdBy 是下属 userId）
1008:       if (snapMindmapIds.size > 0) {
1009:         await tx.relationship.deleteMany({
1010:           where: {
1011:             createdBy: userId,
1012:             mindmapId: { in: [...snapMindmapIds] },
1013:             id: { notIn: snapRelIds.size > 0 ? [...snapRelIds] : [-1] },
1014:           },
1015:         });
1016:       }
1017: 
1018:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1019:       // 10. MentionEvent（仅追加）
1020:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1021:       for (const mention of snap.mentions ?? []) {
1022:         if (!isTempId(mention.id)) continue;
1023:         const nodeDbId = resolveId(mention.nodeId, idMap);
1024:         if (!nodeDbId) continue;
1025:         const created = await tx.mentionEvent.create({
1026:           data: {
1027:             nodeId: nodeDbId,
1028:             byUserId: resolveId(mention.byUserId, idMap) ?? userId,
1029:             mentionedUserId: resolveId(mention.mentionedUserId, idMap) ?? userId,
1030:             kind: mention.kind,
1031:             text: mention.text ?? "",
1032:             dingtalkPushedAt: mention.dingtalkPushedAt
1033:               ? new Date(mention.dingtalkPushedAt)
1034:               : null,
1035:           },
1036:         });
1037:         idMap.set(mention.id, created.id);
1038:       }
1039: 
1040:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1041:       // 11. CalendarSync（upsert by nodeId+provider）
1042:       // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1043:       for (const cs of snap.calendarSyncs ?? []) {
1044:         const nodeDbId = resolveId(cs.nodeId, idMap);
1045:         if (!nodeDbId) continue;
1046:         if (isTempId(cs.id)) {
1047:           const created = await tx.calendarSync.create({
1048:             data: {
1049:               nodeId: nodeDbId,
1050:               userId,
1051:               provider: cs.provider,
1052:               externalEventId: cs.externalEventId,
1053:               syncedTitle: cs.syncedTitle ?? "",
1054:               syncedDeadline: cs.syncedDeadline ?? null,
1055:               syncedStatus: cs.syncedStatus ?? null,
1056:               externalCompleted: cs.externalCompleted ?? false,
1057:               status: cs.status ?? "pending",
1058:               syncedAt: new Date(),
1059:               lastError: cs.lastError ?? null,
1060:             },
1061:           });
1062:           idMap.set(cs.id, created.id);
1063:         } else {
1064:           const dbId = parseDbId(cs.id);
1065:           if (!dbId) continue;
1066:           await tx.calendarSync.updateMany({
1067:             where: { id: dbId, userId },
1068:             data: {
1069:               syncedTitle: cs.syncedTitle ?? "",
1070:               syncedDeadline: cs.syncedDeadline ?? null,
1071:               syncedStatus: cs.syncedStatus ?? null,
1072:               externalCompleted: cs.externalCompleted ?? false,
1073:               status: cs.status ?? "pending",
1074:               syncedAt: new Date(),
1075:               lastError: cs.lastError ?? null,
1076:             },
1077:           });
1078:         }
1079:       }
1080:     },
1081:     { timeout: 30000 },
1082:   );
1083: 
1084:   // 将 Map 转为普通对象，值转为字符串（与前端 string ID 对齐）
1085:   const idMapObj: Record<string, string> = {};
1086:   for (const [tempId, dbId] of idMap.entries()) {
1087:     idMapObj[tempId] = String(dbId);
1088:   }
1089: 
1090:   logger.info(
1091:     { user: userId, method: "PUT", path: "/api/workspace" },
1092:     `快照保存完成，idMap 条目数：${idMap.size}`,
1093:   );
1094: 
1095:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, idMap: idMapObj });
1096: }
1097: 
1098: export const GET = withApiLogger(getHandler);
1099: export const PUT = withApiLogger(putHandler);
1100: 
1101: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1102: // 节点拓扑排序（父节点先于子节点）
1103: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1104: function topoSortNodes<T extends { id: string; parentId?: string | null }>(
1105:   nodes: T[],
1106: ): T[] {
1107:   const result: T[] = [];
1108:   const visited = new Set<string>();
1109:   const map = new Map<string, T>(nodes.map((n) => [n.id, n]));
1110: 
1111:   function visit(node: T) {
1112:     if (visited.has(node.id)) return;
1113:     if (node.parentId && map.has(node.parentId)) {
1114:       visit(map.get(node.parentId)!);
1115:     }
1116:     visited.add(node.id);
1117:     result.push(node);
1118:   }
1119:

</content>

126:         setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === editTarget.id ? (d.user ?? u) : u));
127:         toast.success("用户信息已更新");
128:         // PATCH 总是包含 managerId，可能改变 OrgRelation，刷新全局 relations

130:       } else {

135:         });

145:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
146:     } finally {

316:                 value={form.managerId}
317:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, managerId: e.target.value }))}
318:               >
319:                 <option value="">无上级</option>
320:                 {users
321:                   .filter(u => u.status === "active" && u.id !== editTarget?.id)
322:                   .map(u => (
323:                     <option key={u.id} value={u.id}>
324:                       {u.avatar ? `${u.avatar} ` : ""}{u.name}（{u.employeeNo}）
325:                     </option>
326:                   ))}
327:               </select>
328:             </div>
329:             {!editTarget && (
330:               <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-slate-50 rounded p-2">
331:                 新建用户初始密码为 <span className="font-mono font-semibold">123456</span>，请告知用户登录后及时修改。
332:               </p>
333:             )}
334:           </div>
335:           <DialogFooter>
336:             <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowForm(false)} disabled={saving}>取消</Button>
337:             <Button onClick={handleSave} disabled={saving}>{saving ? "保存中…" : "保存"}</Button>
338:           </DialogFooter>
339:         </DialogContent>
340:       </Dialog>
341: 
342:       {/* 禁用确认对话框 */}
343:       <ConfirmDialog
344:         open={!!disableTarget}
345:         title="禁用用户"
346:         description={`确定要禁用用户「${disableTarget?.name}」吗？禁用后该用户将无法登录。`}
347:         confirmLabel="禁用"
348:         destructive
349:         onConfirm={handleDisable}
350:         onCancel={() => setDisableTarget(null)}
351:       />
352:     </>
353:   );

Looking at the workspace route, notifications are created directly via `tx.appNotification.create()`. I should either collect newly created notifications after the transaction and send them to dingtalk asynchronously, or create a helper function in notify.ts to handle this.

The issue is that notifications are created within a Prisma transaction, so I can't make async HTTP calls inside it. The right approach is to fire-and-forget the dingtalk push after the transaction completes around line 1082. But the task specifically says to add this to `createNotification()` in notify.ts, which doesn't exist yet. I need to clarify whether I should create that function or handle it differently in the transaction flow. I need to examine what data's available in the notifications snapshot to understand what I'm working with. Looking at the transaction code, new notifications get created and stored in `idMap` between lines 944-966, but after the transaction completes I only have the `idMap` reference, not the full notification objects themselves. So I'll collect the newly created notifications in a local array during transaction processing, then use that data afterward to fire off the dingtalk pushes. My plan is to create a helper function in `notify.ts` that handles the dingtalk push logic, then in the workspace route after the transaction, I'll gather the new notifications from `snap.notifications` where they have temp IDs and call this helper in a fire-and-forget manner.

Actually, rereading the requirements more carefully—the task explicitly wants `createNotification()` in `notify.ts` to query the recipient's `dingtalkUserId` and trigger the Dingtalk push directly within that function using fire-and-forget semantics. So the function needs Prisma access to look up the user, then invoke the Dingtalk send without waiting for it.

For the workspace route, I should collect the newly created notifications (those with temporary IDs from the transaction) and iterate through them to call `createNotification()` after the transaction completes but before returning. This ensures all existing call sites to `createNotification()` are covered by the new Dingtalk logic. I'm realizing the transaction constraint makes it tricky to call the push function inline, so the cleanest approach is to collect the notification data during the transaction and then trigger the dingtalk pushes afterward as a fire-and-forget operation. I'll create a helper function in the dingtalk module that handles this, keeping the workspace route focused on the transaction logic while delegating the push responsibility elsewhere.

#### 🔧 Tool: write
**Status:** completed
**Title:** home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/lib/dingtalk.ts

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/lib/dingtalk.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * 钉钉企业内部应用服务层\n *\n * 功能：\n *  1. access_token 获取与模块级缓存（过期前 5 分钟主动刷新）\n *  2. sendDingtalkWorkMessage — 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 类型）\n *  3. pushNotificationToDingtalk — 按数据库 recipientId 查 dingtalkUserId 后推送\n *\n * 设计决策（见 openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/design.md）：\n *  - 推送失败只记录 logger.warn，不抛出异常（静默降级）\n *  - 环境变量缺失时直接跳过，不影响主业务\n *  - 使用旧版 API（oapi.dingtalk.com）发送工作通知，兼容性最好\n */\n\nimport { logger } from \"@/lib/logger\";\nimport { prisma } from \"@/lib/prisma\";\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// access_token 缓存\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ninterface TokenCache {\n  token: string;\n  /** 过期时间戳（毫秒），到期前 5 分钟触发刷新 */\n  expiresAt: number;\n}\n\nlet tokenCache: TokenCache | null = null;\n\n/**\n * 获取钉钉企业 access_token（含模块级缓存，过期前 5 分钟刷新）。\n * 环境变量 DINGTALK_APP_KEY / DINGTALK_APP_SECRET 缺失时返回 null。\n */\nasync function getDingtalkToken(): Promise<string | null> {\n  const appKey = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_KEY;\n  const appSecret = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_SECRET;\n\n  if (!appKey || !appSecret) {\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  const now = Date.now();\n  // 提前 5 分钟（300_000 ms）刷新，避免临界过期\n  if (tokenCache && tokenCache.expiresAt - 300_000 > now) {\n    return tokenCache.token;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const url = `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken?appkey=${encodeURIComponent(appKey)}&appsecret=${encodeURIComponent(appSecret)}`;\n    const res = await fetch(url, { method: \"GET\" });\n    const data = (await res.json()) as {\n      errcode: number;\n      errmsg: string;\n      access_token?: string;\n      expires_in?: number;\n    };\n\n    if (data.errcode !== 0 || !data.access_token) {\n      logger.warn(\n        { service: \"dingtalk\" },\n        `获取钉钉 access_token 失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,\n      );\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    // expires_in 单位为秒，默认 7200\n    const expiresIn = (data.expires_in ?? 7200) * 1000;\n    tokenCache = {\n      token: data.access_token,\n      expiresAt: now + expiresIn,\n    };\n    return tokenCache.token;\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ service: \"dingtalk\", err }, \"请求钉钉 access_token 异常\");\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// 发送工作通知\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/**\n * 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 纯文本类型）。\n *\n * @param dingtalkUserId 钉钉用户 userId 或 unionId（由管理员录入）\n * @param content        消息正文（建议格式：`【工作平台】${title}\\n${body}`）\n *\n * 失败时仅 logger.warn，不抛出异常。\n */\nexport async function sendDingtalkWorkMessage(\n  dingtalkUserId: string,\n  content: string,\n): Promise<void> {\n  const agentIdStr = process.env.DINGTALK_AGENT_ID;\n  if (!agentIdStr) {\n    logger.warn({ service: \"dingtalk\" }, \"DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 未配置，跳过推送\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const agentId = parseInt(agentIdStr, 10);\n  if (isNaN(agentId)) {\n    logger.warn(\n      { service: \"dingtalk\" },\n      `DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 格式无效（非整数）：${agentIdStr}`,\n    );\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const token = await getDingtalkToken();\n  if (!token) {\n    // getDingtalkToken 内部已记录 warn，此处不重复\n    return;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const res = await fetch(\n      `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/message/corpconversation/asyncsend_v2?access_token=${token}`,\n      {\n        method: \"POST\",\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          agent_id: agentId,\n          userid_list: dingtalkUserId,\n          msg: {\n            msgtype: \"text\",\n            text: { content },\n          },\n        }),\n      },\n    );\n\n    const data = (await res.json()) as {\n      errcode: number;\n      errmsg: string;\n    };\n\n    if (data.errcode !== 0) {\n      logger.warn(\n        { service: \"dingtalk\", dingtalkUserId },\n        `钉钉工作通知发送失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,\n      );\n    }\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn(\n      { service: \"dingtalk\", dingtalkUserId, err },\n      \"发送钉钉工作通知异常\",\n    );\n  }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// 按 recipientId 推送通知（供 workspace route 调用）\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport interface PendingDingtalkNotif {\n  recipientId: number;\n  title: string;\n  body?: string | null;\n}\n\n/**\n * 批量推送待发钉钉通知（fire-and-forget 场景）。\n *\n * 对每条通知：\n *  1. 查询接收者的 dingtalkUserId\n *  2. 若非空，调用 sendDingtalkWorkMessage\n *\n * 整个函数不抛出异常，失败均 logger.warn 静默处理。\n */\nexport async function pushPendingDingtalkNotifs(\n  notifs: PendingDingtalkNotif[],\n): Promise<void> {\n  if (notifs.length === 0) return;\n\n  // 去重 recipientId，批量查询\n  const recipientIds = [...new Set(notifs.map((n) => n.recipientId))];\n\n  let userMap: Map<number, string>;\n  try {\n    const users = await prisma.user.findMany({\n      where: {\n        id: { in: recipientIds },\n        dingtalkUserId: { not: null },\n      },\n      select: { id: true, dingtalkUserId: true },\n    });\n    userMap = new Map(\n      users\n        .filter((u) => u.dingtalkUserId)\n        .map((u) => [u.id, u.dingtalkUserId!]),\n    );\n  } catch (err) {\n    logger.warn({ service: \"dingtalk\", err }, \"查询用户 dingtalkUserId 异常，跳过推送\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // 逐条推送（不并发，避免触发钉钉限流）\n  for (const notif of notifs) {\n    const dingtalkUserId = userMap.get(notif.recipientId);\n    if (!dingtalkUserId) continue;\n\n    const content = notif.body\n      ? `【工作平台】${notif.title}\\n${notif.body}`\n      : `【工作平台】${notif.title}`;\n\n    // fire-and-forget：不 await，不阻塞调用方\n    void sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId, content);\n  }\n}\n"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.

#### 🔧 Tool: read
**Status:** completed
**Title:** home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/app/api/workspace/route.ts

```json

  "filePath": "/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/app/api/workspace/route.ts",

}
```

**Output:**
```
<path>/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/app/api/workspace/route.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: /**
2:  * GET  /api/workspace  → 获取当前用户的完整工作区快照
3:  * PUT  /api/workspace  → 保存（全量快照 upsert+delete）工作区，返回 idMap
4:  *
5:  * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
6:  * 规范 4-2：所有查询附带 userId 条件，防止越权
7:  * 规范 4-3：getAuth 验证身份
8:  *
9:  * PUT 核心逻辑：
10:  *  1. 字符串临时 ID（前端新建）→ INSERT，记录到 idMap
11:  *  2. 数字 ID → UPDATE（附带 userId 条件）
12:  *  3. DB 中属于当前用户、但快照中不存在的记录 → 软删除
13:  *  4. 跳过空节点（title 为空白）及其所有级联引用
14:  *  5. 返回 { ok: true, idMap: { "n-abc": "12345" } }
15:  */
16: 
17: import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
18: import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
19: import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
20: import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
21: import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";

1: # M-08 用户管理
2: 
3: **状态：** `ACTIVE`
4: 
5: ---
6: 
7: ## 概述
8: 
9: 用户管理模块供系统管理员（`isAdmin=true`）维护用户账号。支持创建用户（含指定直接上级）、编辑基本信息、禁用/启用账号。新建用户初始密码固定为 `123456` 并自动标记 `mustResetPassword=true`，用户首次登录时系统强制跳转重置密码页面。用户禁用为软删除（`status='disabled'`），不物理删除记录。
10: 
11: ---
12: 
13: ## 数据模型
14: 
15: **表：`users`**
16: 
17: | 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
18: |------|------|------|
19: | `id` | INT AUTO_INCREMENT | 主键 |
20: | `employeeNo` | VARCHAR | 工号，全局唯一，创建后不可修改 |
21: | `name` | VARCHAR | 姓名 |
22: | `email` | VARCHAR | 邮箱，可留空由系统自动生成 `{employeeNo}@company.local` |
23: | `avatar` | VARCHAR / NULL | 头像（emoji 或 URL），可为空 |
24: | `departmentId` | INT | 所属部门外键，必填 |
25: | `jobTitle` | VARCHAR | 职位，必填 |
26: | `passwordHash` | VARCHAR | bcrypt 哈希（cost=12） |
27: | `status` | VARCHAR | 账号状态：`active`（正常）/ `disabled`（已禁用） |
28: | `isAdmin` | BOOLEAN | 是否为管理员，默认 false；新建用户默认 false |
29: | `dingtalkBound` | BOOLEAN | 是否绑定钉钉，默认 false |
30: | `managerId` | INT / NULL | 直接上级用户 ID（自引用外键），可为空 |
31: | `mustResetPassword` | BOOLEAN | 是否需要重置密码，新建用户默认 true，重置后置 false |
32: | `createdAt` / `updatedAt` | DATETIME | 北京时间（UTC+8） |
33: 
34: ---

37: 
38: 所有接口需携带 `Authorization: Bearer <JWT>` 请求头，且调用方必须为管理员（`isAdmin=true`），否则返回 403。

<path>/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/.specs/modules/M-08-user-mgmt.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
50:         "email": "zhangsan@company.com",
51:         "avatar": "👤",
52:         "departmentId": "1",
53:         "jobTitle": "产品经理",
54:         "status": "active",
55:         "isAdmin": false,
56:         "dingtalkBound": false
57:       }
58:     ]
59:   }
60:   ```
61: - **说明：** 返回所有用户（含已禁用），按 id 升序。`id`/`departmentId` 序列化为字符串。
62: 
63: ### POST /api/admin/users
64: - **权限：** 管理员
65: - **入参（JSON Body）：**
66: 
67:   | 字段 | 必填 | 说明 |
68:   |------|------|------|
69:   | `employeeNo` | 是 | 工号，必须唯一 |
70:   | `name` | 是 | 姓名 |
71:   | `departmentId` | 是 | 部门 ID（字符串） |
72:   | `jobTitle` | 是 | 职位 |
73:   | `email` | 否 | 邮箱，留空自动生成 |
74:   | `avatar` | 否 | 头像 emoji |
75:   | `managerId` | 否 | 直接上级用户 ID（字符串） |
76: 
77: - **出参：** `{ "user": { ...同上 } }`，HTTP 201
78: - **说明：** 新建用户自动设置 `mustResetPassword=true`，初始密码为 `123456`（bcrypt 哈希存储）。
79: - **错误：** 400（参数缺失/上级不存在）、409（工号已存在）
80: 
81: ### PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]
82: - **权限：** 管理员
83: - **入参（JSON Body，所有字段可选）：** `name`, `email`, `avatar`, `departmentId`, `jobTitle`, `status`, `isAdmin`, `managerId`（传 `null` 或空字符串表示清除上级）
84: - **业务规则：**
85:   - 不能将自己的 `isAdmin` 改为 false（防止系统锁死）
86:   - 部门 ID 会做存在性校验
87: - **出参：** `{ "user": { ...同上 } }`
88: 
89: ### DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]
90: - **权限：** 管理员
91: - **操作：** 软删除，将 `status` 改为 `disabled`
92: - **业务规则：** 不能禁用自己的账号
93: - **出参：** `{ "ok": true }`
94: 
95: ---
96: 
97: ## 业务逻辑
98: 
99: 1. **工号唯一性**：`POST` 创建时在数据库层做唯一性检查，重复返回 409。
100: 2. **初始密码**：固定为 `123456`，服务端使用 `bcrypt`（cost=12）哈希后存储。新建用户自动设 `mustResetPassword=true`。
101: 3. **首次登录强制重置**：`mustResetPassword=true` 的用户登录后，LoginPage 跳转 `/reset-password`；AppShell 在非 `/reset-password` 页也会强制重定向；重置成功后清除标记、刷新工作区，跳转 `/mindmap`。
102: 4. **直接上级**：新建/编辑时可选择直接上级（下拉仅显示 active 用户），不能将自己设为自己的上级。
103: 5. **软删除**：`DELETE` 将 `status` 设为 `disabled`，`PATCH` 传 `{ status: "active" }` 可恢复。
104: 6. **自身保护**：
105:    - 管理员不能禁用自己（`DELETE` 校验 `targetId === userId`）
106:    - 管理员不能取消自己的 `isAdmin`（`PATCH` 校验 `targetId === userId && isAdmin === false`）
107: 7. **前端权限守卫**：页面加载时检查 `currentUser.isAdmin`，非管理员跳转 `/mindmap`。
108: 
109: ---
110: 
111: ## 前端组件
112: 
113: | 组件 | 路径 | 职责 |
114: |------|------|------|
115: | `AdminUsersPage` | `src/pages/admin/AdminUsersPage.tsx` | 用户列表表格 + 新建/编辑 Dialog（含直接上级下拉）+ 禁用 ConfirmDialog |
116: | `ResetPasswordPage` | `src/pages/ResetPasswordPage.tsx` | 首次登录重置密码表单 |
117: | 路由入口 | `src/app/(app)/admin/users/page.tsx` | 渲染 `AdminUsersPage` |
118: | 路由入口 | `src/app/(app)/reset-password/page.tsx` | 渲染 `ResetPasswordPage` |
119: 
120: **AdminUsersPage 功能：**
121: - 表格展示：工号、姓名、部门（名称）、职位、状态标签、角色标签（管理员徽章）
122: - 新建用户：Dialog 填写工号/姓名/邮箱/头像/部门/职位/**直接上级**，保存成功后 toast 提示初始密码
123: - 编辑用户：打开 Dialog 时自动填充当前数据（规范 1-3），可修改姓名/邮箱/头像/部门/职位/**直接上级**
124: - 禁用用户：`ConfirmDialog` 二次确认，`destructive` 样式，自身账号禁用按钮置灰
125: - 启用用户：直接点击启用图标，无需二次确认
126: 
127: **ResetPasswordPage 功能：**
128: - 输入新密码 + 确认密码（≥6 位，不能与初始密码 `123456` 相同）
129: - 调用 `POST /api/auth/reset-password`，成功后 `refreshWorkspace()` 并跳转 `/mindmap`
130: 
131: ---
132: 
133: ## 变更记录
134: 
135: | 日期 | 编号 | 变更内容 | 原始需求 |
136: |------|------|----------|----------|
137: | 2026-05-19 | T-08-001 | 初始实现用户管理 API（GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE）及前端页面 | 生产化改造——管理员维护用户账号 |
138: | 2026-05-19 | T-08-002 | 新增直接上级（managerId）字段：schema、API、前端下拉 | 添加和编辑用户时需要指定直接上级 |
139: | 2026-05-19 | T-08-003 | 新建用户自动设 mustResetPassword=true；首次登录跳转重置密码页面 | 首次登录时需要跳转到重置密码界面 |
140: | 2026-05-19 | B-08-001 | POST /api/admin/users 新增：创建用户时同步写入 OrgRelation(solid) | 修复申请关注提示"没有上级" |
141: | 2026-05-19 | B-08-002 | PATCH /api/admin/users/[id] 新增：managerId 变更时重建 OrgRelation | 修复申请关注提示"没有上级" |
142: | 2026-05-19 | B-08-003 | AdminUsersPage 保存后调用 refreshWorkspace() 使 relations 立即生效 | 修复申请关注提示"没有上级" |

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Looking at task 6.3: "在 `.specs/MODULES.md` 中登记 `M-10 钉钉通知服务`（若判断需要独立模块）"

The condition says "若判断需要独立模块". Looking at the implementation:
- The dingtalk service is `src/lib/dingtalk.ts` which is a library file
- It's tightly integrated into the notification system (M-07) and user management (M-08)
- It doesn't have its own API endpoints

I think this doesn't need a separate module - it's an extension of existing modules. 

Since there's no dedicated API route for the dingtalk service and it's purely a library integration, I'll skip creating M-10 as a separate module.

</details>

钉钉服务实现为 `src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 纯库层集成（无独立 API 路由），功能已合并进 M-07（通知）和 M-08（用户管理），无需新建独立模块。任务 6.3 按"不需独立模块"判断跳过。

# 变更日志

## [2026-05-20] Bug B-05-011：修复 assigner 侧 mirror 节点未建立及进度不同步

### 修复
- B-05-011 `GET /api/workspace` 新增服务端 reconciliation 块：assigner 每次拉取工作区时，自动遍历已接受且含 `assignerSourceNodeId` 的 assignment；若 source 节点尚无 `taskPeer` 则就地升级（写 DB + 更新 mergedNodes）并同步 `assignerMirrorNodeId`；若已有 `taskPeer` 则仅同步进度字段（status/progressPct/deadline/closedAt）；若 result 节点缺少 executorPeer 则补齐（写 assignee 的节点 DB）

### 变更
- B-05-011 `serializeAssignment` 补充 `assignerSourceNodeId` 序列化（此前字段从未写入 GET 响应，assignee 加载时字段丢失）
- B-05-011 PUT handler assignment CREATE 块追加 `assignerSourceNodeId` 持久化（此前字段从未写入数据库）

## [2026-05-20] 派任务 mirror 节点就地升级 & assignerSourceNodeId 记录

### 新增
- T-05-003 `Assignment` 新增 `assignerSourceNodeId` 字段（`prisma/schema.prisma` + `src/types/index.ts`）：记录派任务时上级选中的源节点 ID，便于后续溯源与 mirror 匹配
- T-05-003 `pairNodesForAssignmentMirror` 返回字段重构：返回类型新增 `isUpgrade: boolean` 和 `assignerMirrorNodeId`；`mirror` 字段重命名为 `mirrorNode`；新增就地升级分支——当源节点为纯普通节点（`!task && !taskPeer`）时，直接在原节点上设置 executor/manager TaskPeerLink 互链，无需新建节点
- T-05-003 `AcceptResult` 新增 `updatedNodes: Node[]`：存放就地升级的已有节点；`attachAssignmentMirror` 按 `isUpgrade` 分支将节点写入 `updatedNodes`（升级）或 `newNodes`（新建）
- T-05-003 `InboxPage.tsx` 新增 `applyAcceptResult` 辅助函数：统一处理 `newNodes`（spread append）和 `updatedNodes`（id 匹配 map replace），`handleAccept` / `handleAcceptAdjustment` 均改用该函数

### 变更

## 实现完成

**变更：** dingtalk-notification  
**Schema：** spec-driven  
**进度：19/19 任务已完成 ✓**

### 本次完成的内容

**数据库层**
- `prisma/schema.prisma` User 模型新增 `dingtalkUserId String?`，已 `db push` 同步到数据库

**钉钉服务层** (`src/lib/dingtalk.ts`)
- access_token 模块级缓存（过期前 5 分钟自动刷新）
- `sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId, content)` — 调用钉钉工作通知 API，失败静默降级
- `pushPendingDingtalkNotifs(notifs)` — 批量按 recipientId 查 dingtalkUserId 后推送

**通知触发** (`src/app/api/workspace/route.ts`)
- 事务中收集新建的 `AppNotification` 数据
- 事务提交后 `void pushPendingDingtalkNotifs(...)` fire-and-forget，不阻塞响应

**用户管理后端** (`src/app/api/admin/users/[id]/route.ts` + `route.ts`)
- `PATCH` 接受 `dingtalkUserId`，自动同步 `dingtalkBound`
- GET/POST/PATCH 响应均包含 `dingtalkUserId` 字段

**用户管理前端** (`src/pages/admin/AdminUsersPage.tsx`)
- `AdminUser` 接口新增 `dingtalkUserId?`
- 编辑 Dialog 新增"钉钉用户 ID"输入框，打开时自动带出当前值

**文档更新**
- M-07、M-08 SDD 变更记录各追加一行
- `.specs/CHANGELOG.md` 追加本次变更条目

**注意**：`db:comments` 脚本因 `mysql2` 包未安装（环境预存问题）无法执行，不影响功能；Prisma schema 已有 `///` 注释覆盖。

{
  "command": "cd /home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend && node -e \"\nconst appKey = 'dingaa5xijzqqvtx0goy';\nconst appSecret = 'yUmLlPujfFkIRrOa2uNW0nPYNWRCuVxRXOfjmWl6s8XENivJltn7tED7COzajuWT';\nconst jobNumbers = ['1168', '3503', 'AH5958', 'AH7407'];\n\nasync function run() {\n  // 1. 获取旧版 token（用于 oapi.dingtalk.com 接口）\n  const tokenRes = await fetch('https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken?appkey=' + appKey + '&appsecret=' + appSecret);\n  const tokenData = await tokenRes.json();\n  if (tokenData.errcode !== 0) { console.error('token error:', tokenData); return; }\n  const oldToken = tokenData.access_token;\n\n  // 2. 获取新版 token（用于 api.dingtalk.com 接口）\n  const newTokenRes = await fetch('https://api.dingtalk.com/v1.0/oauth2/accessToken', {\n    method: 'POST',\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify({ appKey, appSecret })\n  });\n  const newTokenData = await newTokenRes.json();\n  console.log('新版 token result:', JSON.stringify(newTokenData).substring(0, 100));\n  const newToken = newTokenData.accessToken;\n\n  if (!newToken) {\n    console.log('新版 token 获取失败，尝试用旧版接口搜索...');\n    // 尝试用旧版接口按工号查询\n    for (const jn of jobNumbers) {\n      const r = await fetch('https://oapi.dingtalk.com/user/getbyunionid?access_token=' + oldToken + '&unionid=xxx');\n      // 尝试 list API\n      const r2 = await fetch('https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/smartwork/hrm/employee/queryonjob?access_token=' + oldToken, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},\n        body: JSON.stringify({ op_userid: 'admin', status_list: [2], offset: 0, size: 50 })\n      });\n      const d2 = await r2.json();\n      console.log('hrm queryonjob:', JSON.stringify(d2).substring(0, 300));\n      break;\n    }\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // 用新版搜索 API 按工号搜索\n  for (const jn of jobNumbers) {\n    const r = await fetch('https://api.dingtalk.com/v1.0/contact/search', {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-acs-dingtalk-access-token': newToken },\n      body: JSON.stringify({ searchText: jn, searchType: 0, offset: 0, size: 5 })\n    });\n    const d = await r.json();\n    console.log('搜索工号 ' + jn + ':', JSON.stringify(d).substring(0, 400));\n  }\n}\n\nrun().catch(console.error);\n\"",

  "timeout": 30000
}

#### 🔧 Tool: bash
**Status:** completed
**Title:** Recursively search dingtalk users by job number across all departments

**Input:**
```json
{
  "command": "cd /home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend && node -e \"\nconst appKey = 'dingaa5xijzqqvtx0goy';\nconst appSecret = 'yUmLlPujfFkIRrOa2uNW0nPYNWRCuVxRXOfjmWl6s8XENivJltn7tED7COzajuWT';\nconst targetJobNos = new Set(['1168','3503','AH5958','AH7407']);\n\nasync function getToken() {\n  const r = await fetch('https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken?appkey=' + appKey + '&appsecret=' + appSecret);\n  const d = await r.json();\n  return d.access_token;\n}\n\nasync function getUsersInDept(token, deptId, results) {\n  let cursor = 0;\n  while (true) {\n    const r = await fetch('https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/v2/user/list?access_token=' + token, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},\n      body: JSON.stringify({ dept_id: deptId, cursor, size: 50, contains_access_filter: false })\n    });\n    const d = await r.json();\n    if (d.errcode !== 0) break;\n    for (const u of (d.result?.list ?? ### 🤖 Assistant

## Goal
- 为企业工作管理平台实现钉钉通知集成：所有通知场景推送钉钉工作通知，并为现有用户通过钉钉 API 按工号自动补全信息（dingtalkUserId、邮箱、头像）

## Constraints & Preferences
- 钉钉推送失败必须静默降级（仅 `logger.warn`，不影响主业务）
- 推送以 fire-and-forget 方式执行，不 await 阻塞主流程
- `dingtalkUserId` 字段在后端存储；管理员编辑页可见（已实现输入框）
- 钉钉数据优先覆盖本地数据（包括邮箱、头像）
- 未找到钉钉用户时警告但允许继续

## Progress
### Done
- OpenSpec 变更 `dingtalk-notification` 全部 19 个任务已完成
- `prisma/schema.prisma` User 模型新增 `dingtalkUserId String?`，已 `db push` 同步数据库
- `.env.example` 钉钉配置项已取消注释并补充说明
- 新建 `src/lib/dingtalk.ts`：旧版 token 缓存 + `sendDingtalkWorkMessage()` + `pushPendingDingtalkNotifs()`
- `PUT /api/workspace` 事务后 fire-and-forget 推送已插入（收集新建 `AppNotification` → `void pushPendingDingtalkNotifs()`）
- `PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]` 接受 `dingtalkUserId`，自动同步 `dingtalkBound`，响应含 `dingtalkUserId`
- `GET /api/admin/users` + `POST /api/admin/users`：`serializeUser` 已含 `dingtalkUserId`，select 已更新
- `AdminUsersPage.tsx`：`AdminUser` 接口新增 `dingtalkUserId?`，编辑 Dialog 新增"钉钉用户 ID"输入框，打开时自动带出
- SDD 文档已更新（M-07、M-08、CHANGELOG.md）；tasks.md 全部标记 `[x]`
- 现有用户查询完毕：id=2 jojo（工号1168）、id=3 子杰（工号3503）、id=4 乐乐（工号AH5958）、id=5 海宾（工号AH7407），均无 `dingtalkUserId`
- 钉钉 token 可正常获取（旧版 `oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken` 有效，新版 `api.dingtalk.com/v1.0/oauth2/accessToken` 同样有效，token 相同）

### In Progress
- 通过钉钉 API 为现有 4 名用户补充 `dingtalkUserId`、邮箱、头像

### Blocked
- HRM 员工列表接口报权限不足：`errcode=88, sub_code=60011, 缺少 qyapi_hrm_read_user`
- 新版搜索接口 `POST /v1.0/contact/search` 返回 `InvalidAction.NotFound`（接口路径不存在或无权限）

## Key Decisions
- 工作通知发送：旧版 API `oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/message/corpconversation/asyncsend_v2`
- `dingtalkUserId` 非空时自动置 `dingtalkBound=true`，空/null 时置 false
- 钉钉推送触发点：`PUT /api/workspace` 事务提交后、`return NextResponse.json` 前
- 现有用户钉钉信息补充：优先用钉钉接口按工号查询，钉钉数据覆盖本地

## Next Steps
- 尝试其他可用的钉钉通讯录 API 按工号查询用户（如 `GET /v1.0/contact/users` 分页遍历、或旧版 `topapi/v2/user/list`），找到可用接口后批量写入 4 名用户的 dingtalkUserId、邮箱、头像

## Critical Context
- `.env` 已配置：`DINGTALK_APP_KEY=dingaa5xijzqqvtx0goy`、`DINGTALK_AGENT_ID=4596782174`
- 现有非 admin 用户工号：`1168`（jojo, id=2）、`3503`（子杰, id=3）、`AH5958`（乐乐, id=4）、`AH7407`（海宾, id=5）

- `db:comments` 脚本因 `mysql2` 包未安装无法运行（预存环境问题，不影响功能）

## Goal
- 为企业工作管理平台实现钉钉通知集成，并为现有用户通过钉钉 API 按工号自动补全 dingtalkUserId、邮箱、头像

## Constraints & Preferences
- 钉钉推送失败必须静默降级（仅 `logger.warn`，不影响主业务）
- 推送以 fire-and-forget 方式执行，不 await 阻塞主流程
- `dingtalkUserId` 字段在后端存储；管理员编辑页可见（已实现输入框）
- 钉钉数据优先覆盖本地数据（包括邮箱、头像）
- 未找到钉钉用户时警告但允许继续

## Progress
### Done
- OpenSpec 变更 `dingtalk-notification` 全部 19 个任务已完成
- `prisma/schema.prisma` User 模型新增 `dingtalkUserId String?`，已 `db push` 同步数据库
- `.env.example` 钉钉配置项已取消注释并补充说明
- 新建 `src/lib/dingtalk.ts`：旧版 token 缓存 + `sendDingtalkWorkMessage()` + `pushPendingDingtalkNotifs()`
- `PUT /api/workspace` 事务后 fire-and-forget 推送已插入
- `PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]` 接受 `dingtalkUserId`，自动同步 `dingtalkBound`
- `GET /api/admin/users` + `POST /api/admin/users`：`serializeUser` 已含 `dingtalkUserId`
- `AdminUsersPage.tsx`：`AdminUser` 接口新增 `dingtalkUserId?`，编辑 Dialog 新增"钉钉用户 ID"输入框
- SDD 文档已更新（M-07、M-08、CHANGELOG.md）；tasks.md 全部标记 `[x]`
- 通过 `topapi/v2/user/list` 按工号查找，已找到 2 名用户的钉钉信息：

## Key Decisions

**Title:** 遍历741个部门查找 AH5958/AH7407

**Input:**
```json
{
  "command": "TOKEN=4341dafce39c3ef7935423b48b367631\n\npython3 << 'EOF'\nimport urllib.request, json, time, sys\n\nTOKEN = \"4341dafce39c3ef7935423b48b367631\"\nTARGET_JOB_NUMS = {\"AH5958\", \"AH7407\"}\nfound = {}\n\ndef api(url, data=None):\n    req = urllib.request.Request(url)\n    req.add_header(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n    body = json.dumps(data).encode() if data else None\n    with urllib.request.urlopen(req, body, timeout=10) as r:\n        return json.loads(r.read())\n\n# 获取全量部门\nresp = api(f\"https://oapi.dingtalk.com/department/list?access_token={TOKEN}&fetch_child=true&id=1\")\nall_dept_ids = [str(d[\"id\"]) for d in resp.get(\"department\", [])]\nprint(f\"共 {len(all_dept_ids)} 个部门，开始扫描...\", flush=True)\n\n# 加上根部门 1\nall_dept_ids = [\"1\"] + all_dept_ids\n\nfor i, dept_id in enumerate(all_dept_ids):\n    if len(found) == len(TARGET_JOB_NUMS):\n        break\n    cursor = 0\n    while True:\n        try:\n            r = api(f\"https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/v2/user/list?access_token={TOKEN}\", {\n                \"dept_id\": int(dept_id),\n                \"cursor\": cursor,\n                \"size\": 100,\n                \"order_field\": \"custom\",\n                \"contain_access_limit\": False,\n                \"language\": \"zh_CN\"\n            })\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"  dept {dept_id} 异常: {e}\", flush=True)\n            break\n\n        if r.get(\"errcode\", 0) != 0:\n            break\n\n        page = r.get(\"result\", {})\n        users = page.get(\"list\", [])\n        for u in users:\n            jn = u.get(\"job_number\", \"\")\n            if jn in TARGET_JOB_NUMS and jn not in found:\n                found[jn] = {\n                    \"userid\": u.get(\"userid\"),\n                    \"name\": u.get(\"name\"),\n                    \"email\": u.get(\"email\") or u.get(\"org_email\"),\n                    \"avatar\": u.get(\"avatar\"),\n                    \"dept_id\": dept_id\n                }\n                print(f\"[FOUND] 工号={jn} name={u.get('name')} userid={u.get('userid')} email={u.get('email') or u.get('org_email')}\", flush=True)\n\n        if not page.get(\"has_more\"):\n            break\n        cursor = page.get(\"next_cursor\", cursor + 100)\n\n    if i % 50 == 0:\n        print(f\"  进度: {i}/{len(all_dept_ids)}, 已找到: {list(found.keys())}\", flush=True)\n\nprint(\"\\n=== 最终结果 ===\")\nprint(json.dumps(found, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))\nEOF",
  "description": "遍历741个部门查找 AH5958/AH7407",
  "timeout": 300000
}

/**
 * POST /api/auth/login
 * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
 * 规范 4-3：工号 + 密码登录，bcrypt 校验；失败统一"工号或密码错误"防枚举；
 *           in-memory rate limiting（5 次/分钟/IP）
 *
 * 请求体：{ employeeNo: string, password: string }
 * 响应：{ token: string, user: { id, name, employeeNo } }
 */

import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
import { signToken, verifyPassword } from "@/lib/auth";
import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";

// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// in-memory rate limiting（IP → { count, resetAt }）
// 规范 4-3：登录接口须做频率限制，防止暴力破解
// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const MAX_ATTEMPTS = 5;
const WINDOW_MS = 60 * 1000; // 1 分钟
const ipAttempts = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();

function checkRateLimit(ip: string): boolean {
  const now = Date.now();
  const record = ipAttempts.get(ip);
  if (!record || record.resetAt < now) {
    ipAttempts.set(ip, { count: 1, resetAt: now + WINDOW_MS });
    return true; // 允许
  }
  if (record.count >= MAX_ATTEMPTS) return false; // 超限
  record.count++;
  return true;
}

// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 请求处理
// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function handler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {

```

## 1. `src/lib/dingtalk.ts`（共 210 行）

```ts
/**
 * 钉钉企业内部应用服务层
 *
 * 功能：
 *  1. access_token 获取与模块级缓存（过期前 5 分钟主动刷新）
 *  2. sendDingtalkWorkMessage — 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 类型）
 *  3. pushNotificationToDingtalk — 按数据库 recipientId 查 dingtalkUserId 后推送
 *
 * 设计决策（见 openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/design.md）：
 *  - 推送失败只记录 logger.warn，不抛出异常（静默降级）
 *  - 环境变量缺失时直接跳过，不影响主业务
 *  - 使用旧版 API（oapi.dingtalk.com）发送工作通知，兼容性最好
 */

import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";
import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";

// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// access_token 缓存
// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

interface TokenCache {
  token: string;
  /** 过期时间戳（毫秒），到期前 5 分钟触发刷新 */
  expiresAt: number;
}

let tokenCache: TokenCache | null = null;

/**
 * 获取钉钉企业 access_token（含模块级缓存，过期前 5 分钟刷新）。
 * 环境变量 DINGTALK_APP_KEY / DINGTALK_APP_SECRET 缺失时返回 null。
 */
async function getDingtalkToken(): Promise<string | null> {
  const appKey = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_KEY;
  const appSecret = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_SECRET;

  if (!appKey || !appSecret) {
    return null;
  }

  const now = Date.now();
  // 提前 5 分钟（300_000 ms）刷新，避免临界过期
  if (tokenCache && tokenCache.expiresAt - 300_000 > now) {
    return tokenCache.token;
  }

  try {
    const url = `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken?appkey=${encodeURIComponent(appKey)}&appsecret=${encodeURIComponent(appSecret)}`;
    const res = await fetch(url, { method: "GET" });
    const data = (await res.json()) as {
      errcode: number;
      errmsg: string;
      access_token?: string;
      expires_in?: number;
    };

    if (data.errcode !== 0 || !data.access_token) {
      logger.warn(
        { service: "dingtalk" },
        `获取钉钉 access_token 失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,
      );
      return null;
    }

    // expires_in 单位为秒，默认 7200
    const expiresIn = (data.expires_in ?? 7200) * 1000;
    tokenCache = {
      token: data.access_token,
      expiresAt: now + expiresIn,
    };
    return tokenCache.token;
  } catch (err) {
    logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk", err }, "请求钉钉 access_token 异常");
    return null;
  }
}

// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 发送工作通知
// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 纯文本类型）。
 *
 * @param dingtalkUserId 钉钉用户 userId 或 unionId（由管理员录入）
 * @param content        消息正文（建议格式：`【工作平台】${title}\n${body}`）
 *
 * 失败时仅 logger.warn，不抛出异常。
 */
export async function sendDingtalkWorkMessage(
  dingtalkUserId: string,
  content: string,
): Promise<void> {
  const agentIdStr = process.env.DINGTALK_AGENT_ID;
  if (!agentIdStr) {
    logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk" }, "DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 未配置，跳过推送");
    return;
  }

  const agentId = parseInt(agentIdStr, 10);
  if (isNaN(agentId)) {
    logger.warn(
      { service: "dingtalk" },
      `DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 格式无效（非整数）：${agentIdStr}`,
    );
    return;
  }

  const token = await getDingtalkToken();
  if (!token) {
    // getDingtalkToken 内部已记录 warn，此处不重复
    return;
  }

  try {
    const res = await fetch(
      `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/message/corpconversation/asyncsend_v2?access_token=${token}`,
      {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          agent_id: agentId,
          userid_list: dingtalkUserId,
          msg: {
            msgtype: "text",
            text: { content },
          },
        }),
      },
    );

    const data = (await res.json()) as {
      errcode: number;
      errmsg: string;
    };

    if (data.errcode !== 0) {
      logger.warn(
        { service: "dingtalk", dingtalkUserId },
        `钉钉工作通知发送失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,
      );
    }
  } catch (err) {
    logger.warn(
      { service: "dingtalk", dingtalkUserId, err },
      "发送钉钉工作通知异常",
    );
  }
}

// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 按 recipientId 推送通知（供 workspace route 调用）
// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface PendingDingtalkNotif {
  recipientId: number;
  title: string;
  body?: string | null;
}

/**
 * 批量推送待发钉钉通知（fire-and-forget 场景）。
 *
 * 对每条通知：
 *  1. 查询接收者的 dingtalkUserId
 *  2. 若非空，调用 sendDingtalkWorkMessage
 *
 * 整个函数不抛出异常，失败均 logger.warn 静默处理。
 */
export async function pushPendingDingtalkNotifs(
  notifs: PendingDingtalkNotif[],
): Promise<void> {
  if (notifs.length === 0) return;

  // 去重 recipientId，批量查询
  const recipientIds = [...new Set(notifs.map((n) => n.recipientId))];

  let userMap: Map<number, string>;
  try {
    const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: {
        id: { in: recipientIds },
        dingtalkUserId: { not: null },
      },
      select: { id: true, dingtalkUserId: true },
    });
    userMap = new Map(
      users
        .filter((u) => u.dingtalkUserId)
        .map((u) => [u.id, u.dingtalkUserId!]),
    );
  } catch (err) {
    logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk", err }, "查询用户 dingtalkUserId 异常，跳过推送");
    return;
  }

  // 逐条推送（不并发，避免触发钉钉限流）
  for (const notif of notifs) {
    const dingtalkUserId = userMap.get(notif.recipientId);
    if (!dingtalkUserId) continue;

    const content = notif.body
      ? `【工作平台】${notif.title}\n${notif.body}`
      : `【工作平台】${notif.title}`;

    // fire-and-forget：不 await，不阻塞调用方
    void sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId, content);
  }
}
```

---

## 2. `src/app/api/admin/users/[id]/route.ts`（共 194 行）

```ts
/**
 * PATCH  /api/admin/users/[id]  — 更新用户信息（仅管理员）
 * DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]  — 禁用用户（软删除，仅管理员）
 *
 * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
 * 规范 4-2：操作前校验 isAdmin，且禁止管理员禁用自身
 */

import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";

// ── PATCH ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function patchHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
  const { userId } = await getAuth(req);

  const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
  if (!me?.isAdmin) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
  }

  const targetId = parseInt((ctx?.params as Record<string, string>)?.id ?? "");
  if (isNaN(targetId)) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  const target = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: targetId } });
  if (!target) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 });
  }

  const body = (await req.json()) as {
    name?: string;
    email?: string;
    avatar?: string;
    departmentId?: string;
    jobTitle?: string;
    status?: string;
    isAdmin?: boolean;
    managerId?: string | null;
    dingtalkUserId?: string | null;
  };

  // 部门存在性校验
  if (body.departmentId !== undefined) {
    const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(body.departmentId) } });
    if (!dept) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
    }
  }

  // 直接上级存在性校验
  let managerDbId: number | null | undefined = undefined;
  if (body.managerId !== undefined) {
    if (body.managerId === null || body.managerId === "") {
      managerDbId = null;
    } else {
      const mid = parseInt(body.managerId);
      if (isNaN(mid)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
      if (mid === targetId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能将自己设为自己的上级" }, { status: 400 });
      const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: mid } });
      if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
      managerDbId = mid;
    }
  }

  // 禁止把自己的 isAdmin 去掉（防止锁死系统）
  if (targetId === userId && body.isAdmin === false) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能取消自己的管理员权限" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  const updated = await prisma.user.update({
    where: { id: targetId },
    data: {
      ...(body.name !== undefined && { name: body.name.trim() }),
      ...(body.email !== undefined && { email: body.email.trim() }),
      ...(body.avatar !== undefined && { avatar: body.avatar.trim() || null }),
      ...(body.departmentId !== undefined && { departmentId: parseInt(body.departmentId) }),
      ...(body.jobTitle !== undefined && { jobTitle: body.jobTitle.trim() }),
      ...(body.status !== undefined && { status: body.status }),
      ...(body.isAdmin !== undefined && { isAdmin: body.isAdmin }),
      ...(managerDbId !== undefined && { managerId: managerDbId }),
      // dingtalkUserId：非空字符串→写入并置 dingtalkBound=true；空/null→清空并置 dingtalkBound=false
      ...(body.dingtalkUserId !== undefined && {
        dingtalkUserId: body.dingtalkUserId?.trim() || null,
        dingtalkBound: !!(body.dingtalkUserId?.trim()),
      }),
    },
    select: {
      id: true,
      employeeNo: true,
      name: true,
      email: true,
      avatar: true,
      departmentId: true,
      jobTitle: true,
      status: true,
      isAdmin: true,
      dingtalkBound: true,
      dingtalkUserId: true,
      managerId: true,
      mustResetPassword: true,
    },
  });

  // 同步 OrgRelation：managerId 字段有变更时，重建实线汇报关系
  if (managerDbId !== undefined) {
    // 删除该用户现有的所有实线上级关系
    await prisma.orgRelation.deleteMany({
      where: { subordinateId: targetId, relationType: "solid" },
    });
    if (managerDbId !== null) {
      const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
      await prisma.orgRelation.create({
        data: {
          subordinateId: targetId,
          managerId: managerDbId,
          relationType: "solid",
          effectiveFrom: today,
          effectiveTo: null,
        },
      });
      logger.info(
        { user: userId },
        `同步 OrgRelation：用户 ${targetId} → 新上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
      );
    } else {
      logger.info(
        { user: userId },
        `同步 OrgRelation：清除用户 ${targetId} 的实线上级关系`,
      );
    }
  }

  logger.info({ user: userId }, `管理员更新用户 ${targetId}：${JSON.stringify(body)}`);

  return NextResponse.json({
    user: {
      id: String(updated.id),
      employeeNo: updated.employeeNo,
      name: updated.name,
      email: updated.email,
      avatar: updated.avatar ?? undefined,
      departmentId: String(updated.departmentId),
      jobTitle: updated.jobTitle,
      status: updated.status,
      isAdmin: updated.isAdmin,
      dingtalkBound: updated.dingtalkBound,
      dingtalkUserId: updated.dingtalkUserId ?? undefined,
      managerId: updated.managerId ? String(updated.managerId) : undefined,
      mustResetPassword: updated.mustResetPassword,
    },
  });
}

// ── DELETE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function deleteHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
  const { userId } = await getAuth(req);

  const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
  if (!me?.isAdmin) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
  }

  const targetId = parseInt((ctx?.params as Record<string, string>)?.id ?? "");
  if (isNaN(targetId)) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  // 禁止管理员删除自身
  if (targetId === userId) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能禁用自己的账号" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  const target = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: targetId } });
  if (!target) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 });
  }

  // 软删除：状态改为 disabled
  await prisma.user.update({
    where: { id: targetId },
    data: { status: "disabled" },
  });

  logger.info({ user: userId }, `管理员禁用用户 ${targetId}（${target.employeeNo} ${target.name}）`);

  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true });
}

export const PATCH = withApiLogger(patchHandler);
export const DELETE = withApiLogger(deleteHandler);
```

## 3. `src/pages/admin/AdminUsersPage.tsx`（共 369 行）

```tsx
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import PageHeader from "@/components/PageHeader";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogFooter,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { ConfirmDialog } from "@/components/ui/ConfirmDialog";
import { toast } from "@/store/toast";
import { getApiToken } from "@/lib/api/workspaceApi";
import { useStore } from "@/store/StoreProvider";
import { UserPlus, Pencil, Ban, CheckCircle2 } from "lucide-react";

interface AdminUser {
  id: string;
  employeeNo: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  departmentId: string;
  jobTitle: string;
  status: string;
  isAdmin: boolean;
  managerId?: string;
  dingtalkUserId?: string;
}

interface Dept {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  parentId?: string;
}

function authHeaders() {
  return { "Content-Type": "application/json", Authorization: `Bearer ${getApiToken()}` };
}

export default function AdminUsersPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { currentUser, refreshWorkspace } = useStore();

  const [users, setUsers] = useState<AdminUser[]>([]);
  const [depts, setDepts] = useState<Dept[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  // 新建/编辑对话框
  const [showForm, setShowForm] = useState(false);
  const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "", dingtalkUserId: "" });
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);

  // 禁用确认
  const [disableTarget, setDisableTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);

  // 权限检查
  useEffect(() => {
    if (currentUser && !currentUser.isAdmin) {
      router.replace("/mindmap");
    }
  }, [currentUser, router]);

  const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [uRes, dRes] = await Promise.all([
        fetch("/api/admin/users", { headers: authHeaders() }),
        fetch("/api/admin/departments", { headers: authHeaders() }),
      ]);
      const uJson = await uRes.json() as { users?: AdminUser[]; error?: string };
      const dJson = await dRes.json() as { departments?: Dept[]; error?: string };
      if (!uRes.ok) throw new Error(uJson.error ?? "加载用户失败");
      if (!dRes.ok) throw new Error(dJson.error ?? "加载部门失败");
      setUsers(uJson.users ?? []);
      setDepts(dJson.departments ?? []);
    } catch (e) {
      toast.error((e as Error).message);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { void fetchData(); }, [fetchData]);

  function openCreate() {
    setEditTarget(null);
    setForm({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: depts[0]?.id ?? "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "", dingtalkUserId: "" });
    setShowForm(true);
  }

  function openEdit(u: AdminUser) {
    setEditTarget(u);
    setForm({ employeeNo: u.employeeNo, name: u.name, email: u.email, avatar: u.avatar ?? "", departmentId: u.departmentId, jobTitle: u.jobTitle, managerId: u.managerId ?? "", dingtalkUserId: u.dingtalkUserId ?? "" });
    setShowForm(true);
  }

  async function handleSave() {
    if (!form.name.trim()) { toast.error("姓名不能为空"); return; }
    if (!form.departmentId) { toast.error("请选择部门"); return; }
    if (!form.jobTitle.trim()) { toast.error("职位不能为空"); return; }
    if (!editTarget && !form.employeeNo.trim()) { toast.error("工号不能为空"); return; }

    setSaving(true);
    try {
      if (editTarget) {
        const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${editTarget.id}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          headers: authHeaders(),
          body: JSON.stringify({
            name: form.name,
            email: form.email,
            avatar: form.avatar,
            departmentId: form.departmentId,
            jobTitle: form.jobTitle,
            managerId: form.managerId || null,
            dingtalkUserId: form.dingtalkUserId.trim() || null,
          }),
        });
        const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
        if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "更新失败");
        setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === editTarget.id ? (d.user ?? u) : u));
        toast.success("用户信息已更新");
        // PATCH 总是包含 managerId，可能改变 OrgRelation，刷新全局 relations
        void refreshWorkspace();
      } else {
        const r = await fetch("/api/admin/users", {
          method: "POST",
          headers: authHeaders(),
          body: JSON.stringify({ ...form, managerId: form.managerId || undefined }),
        });
        const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
        if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "创建失败");
        setUsers(prev => [...prev, d.user!]);
        toast.success(`用户 ${form.name} 创建成功，初始密码：123456`);
        // 新用户若有直属上级，刷新全局 relations
        if (form.managerId) void refreshWorkspace();
      }
      setShowForm(false);
    } catch (e) {
      toast.error((e as Error).message);
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleDisable() {
    if (!disableTarget) return;
    try {
      const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${disableTarget.id}`, {
        method: "DELETE",
        headers: authHeaders(),
      });
      const d = await r.json() as { ok?: boolean; error?: string };
      if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
      setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === disableTarget.id ? { ...u, status: "disabled" } : u));
      toast.success(`用户 ${disableTarget.name} 已禁用`);
    } catch (e) {
      toast.error((e as Error).message);
    } finally {
      setDisableTarget(null);
    }
  }

  async function handleEnable(u: AdminUser) {
    try {
      const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}`, {
        method: "PATCH",
        headers: authHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ status: "active" }),
      });
      const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
      if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
      setUsers(prev => prev.map(usr => usr.id === u.id ? { ...usr, status: "active" } : usr));
      toast.success(`用户 ${u.name} 已启用`);
    } catch (e) {
      toast.error((e as Error).message);
    }
  }

  function deptName(id: string) {
    return depts.find(d => d.id === id)?.name ?? id;
  }

  return (
    <>
      <PageHeader
        title="用户管理"
        description="管理系统用户账号，新建用户初始密码为 123456"
        right={
          <Button onClick={openCreate} size="sm">
            <UserPlus className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
            新建用户
          </Button>
        }
      />

      <div className="flex-1 p-6 overflow-auto">
        {loading ? (
          <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">加载中…</div>
        ) : (
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-border overflow-hidden">
            <table className="w-full text-sm">
              <thead className="bg-slate-50 border-b border-border">
                <tr>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">工号</th>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">姓名</th>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">部门</th>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">职位</th>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">状态</th>
                  <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">角色</th>
                  <th className="text-right px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">操作</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="divide-y divide-border">
                {users.map(u => (
                  <tr key={u.id} className="hover:bg-slate-50">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{u.employeeNo}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 font-medium text-brand-ink">
                      {u.avatar ? <span className="mr-1">{u.avatar}</span> : null}
                      {u.name}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{deptName(u.departmentId)}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{u.jobTitle}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${u.status === "active" ? "bg-green-50 text-green-700" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-500"}`}>
                        {u.status === "active" ? "正常" : "已禁用"}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {u.isAdmin && (
                        <span className="inline-flex px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-orange-50 text-orange-700">管理员</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">
                        <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => openEdit(u)} title="编辑">
                          <Pencil className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                        </Button>
                        {u.status === "active" ? (
                          <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => setDisableTarget(u)} title="禁用" disabled={u.id === currentUser?.id}>
                            <Ban className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-destructive" />
                          </Button>
                        ) : (
                          <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => handleEnable(u)} title="启用">
                            <CheckCircle2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-600" />
                          </Button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
                {users.length === 0 && (
                  <tr>
                    <td colSpan={7} className="px-4 py-10 text-center text-muted-foreground">
                      暂无用户，请点击右上角新建
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 新建/编辑对话框 */}
      <Dialog open={showForm} onOpenChange={setShowForm}>
        <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>{editTarget ? "编辑用户" : "新建用户"}</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
            {!editTarget && (
              <div className="space-y-1.5">
                <Label>工号 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
                <Input value={form.employeeNo} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, employeeNo: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 E011" />
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>姓名 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <Input value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, name: e.target.value }))} placeholder="真实姓名" />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>邮箱</Label>
              <Input value={form.email} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, email: e.target.value }))} placeholder="可留空，自动生成" type="email" />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>头像（emoji）</Label>
              <Input value={form.avatar} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, avatar: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 👤（可留空）" />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>部门 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <select
                className="w-full border border-input rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-background"
                value={form.departmentId}
                onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, departmentId: e.target.value }))}
              >
                <option value="">请选择部门</option>
                {depts.map(d => (
                  <option key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>职位 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <Input value={form.jobTitle} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, jobTitle: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 产品经理" />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label>直接上级</Label>
              <select
                className="w-full border border-input rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-background"
                value={form.managerId}
                onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, managerId: e.target.value }))}
              >
                <option value="">无上级</option>
                {users
                  .filter(u => u.status === "active" && u.id !== editTarget?.id)
                  .map(u => (
                    <option key={u.id} value={u.id}>
                      {u.avatar ? `${u.avatar} ` : ""}{u.name}（{u.employeeNo}）
                    </option>
                  ))}
              </select>
            </div>
            {editTarget && (
              <div className="space-y-1.5">
                <Label>钉钉用户 ID</Label>
                <Input
                  value={form.dingtalkUserId}
                  onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, dingtalkUserId: e.target.value }))}
                  placeholder="由管理员录入，用于推送工作通知（可留空）"
                />
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  填入后系统将向该用户钉钉账号推送工作通知；留空则不推送。
                </p>
              </div>
            )}
            {!editTarget && (
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-slate-50 rounded p-2">
                新建用户初始密码为 <span className="font-mono font-semibold">123456</span>，请告知用户登录后及时修改。
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <DialogFooter>
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowForm(false)} disabled={saving}>取消</Button>
            <Button onClick={handleSave} disabled={saving}>{saving ? "保存中…" : "保存"}</Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      {/* 禁用确认对话框 */}
      <ConfirmDialog
        open={!!disableTarget}
        title="禁用用户"
        description={`确定要禁用用户「${disableTarget?.name}」吗？禁用后该用户将无法登录。`}
        confirmLabel="禁用"
        destructive
        onConfirm={handleDisable}
        onCancel={() => setDisableTarget(null)}
      />
    </>
  );
}
```

## 4. `src/app/api/admin/users/route.ts`（共 191 行）

```ts
/**
 * GET  /api/admin/users  — 查询用户列表（仅管理员）
 * POST /api/admin/users  — 创建用户，初始密码固定为 123456（仅管理员）
 *
 * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
 * 规范 4-2：操作前校验 isAdmin
 * 规范 4-3：getAuth 鉴权
 */

import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
import { hashPassword } from "@/lib/auth";
import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";

/** 初始密码（管理员创建用户时使用，用户首次登录后应自行修改） */
const INITIAL_PASSWORD = "123456";

// ── 工具：序列化用户行 ──────────────────────────────────────────
function serializeUser(u: {
  id: number;
  employeeNo: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar: string | null;
  departmentId: number;
  jobTitle: string;
  status: string;
  isAdmin: boolean;
  dingtalkBound: boolean;
  dingtalkUserId: string | null;
  managerId: number | null;
  mustResetPassword: boolean;
}) {
  return {
    id: String(u.id),
    employeeNo: u.employeeNo,
    name: u.name,
    email: u.email,
    avatar: u.avatar ?? undefined,
    departmentId: String(u.departmentId),
    jobTitle: u.jobTitle,
    status: u.status,
    isAdmin: u.isAdmin,
    dingtalkBound: u.dingtalkBound,
    dingtalkUserId: u.dingtalkUserId ?? undefined,
    managerId: u.managerId ? String(u.managerId) : undefined,
    mustResetPassword: u.mustResetPassword,
  };
}

// ── GET ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function getHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
  const { userId } = await getAuth(req);

  const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
  if (!me?.isAdmin) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可访问" }, { status: 403 });
  }

  const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
    orderBy: { id: "asc" },
    select: {
      id: true,
      employeeNo: true,
      name: true,
      email: true,
      avatar: true,
      departmentId: true,
      jobTitle: true,
      status: true,
      isAdmin: true,
      dingtalkBound: true,
      dingtalkUserId: true,
      managerId: true,
      mustResetPassword: true,
    },
  });

  return NextResponse.json({ users: users.map(serializeUser) });
}

// ── POST ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function postHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
  const { userId } = await getAuth(req);

  const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
  if (!me?.isAdmin) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
  }

  const body = (await req.json()) as {
    employeeNo?: string;
    name?: string;
    email?: string;
    departmentId?: string;
    jobTitle?: string;
    avatar?: string;
    managerId?: string;
  };

  const { employeeNo, name, email, departmentId, jobTitle, avatar, managerId } = body;

  if (!employeeNo?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
  if (!name?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "姓名不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
  if (!departmentId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
  if (!jobTitle?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "职位不能为空" }, { status: 400 });

  // 工号唯一性校验
  const existing = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { employeeNo: employeeNo.trim() } });
  if (existing) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号已存在" }, { status: 409 });
  }

  // 部门存在性校验（规范 4-2：后端独立鉴权，不信任前端传值）
  const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(departmentId) } });
  if (!dept) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  // 直接上级存在性校验（如果指定）
  let managerDbId: number | null = null;
  if (managerId) {
    managerDbId = parseInt(managerId);
    if (isNaN(managerDbId)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
    const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: managerDbId } });
    if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
  }

  const passwordHash = await hashPassword(INITIAL_PASSWORD);

  const created = await prisma.user.create({
    data: {
      employeeNo: employeeNo.trim(),
      name: name.trim(),
      email: email?.trim() || `${employeeNo.trim()}@company.local`,
      avatar: avatar?.trim() || null,
      departmentId: parseInt(departmentId),
      jobTitle: jobTitle.trim(),
      status: "active",
      passwordHash,
      isAdmin: false,
      managerId: managerDbId,
      mustResetPassword: true,
    },
    select: {
      id: true,
      employeeNo: true,
      name: true,
      email: true,
      avatar: true,
      departmentId: true,
      jobTitle: true,
      status: true,
      isAdmin: true,
      dingtalkBound: true,
      dingtalkUserId: true,
      managerId: true,
      mustResetPassword: true,
    },
  });

  // 同步 OrgRelation：若设置了直属上级，创建实线汇报关系
  if (managerDbId) {
    const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    await prisma.orgRelation.create({
      data: {
        subordinateId: created.id,
        managerId: managerDbId,
        relationType: "solid",
        effectiveFrom: today,
        effectiveTo: null,
      },
    });
    logger.info(
      { user: userId },
      `同步 OrgRelation：新用户 ${created.id} → 上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
    );
  }

  logger.info(
    { user: userId },
    `管理员创建用户：${created.employeeNo} ${created.name}`,
  );

  return NextResponse.json({ user: serializeUser(created) }, { status: 201 });
}

export const GET = withApiLogger(getHandler);
export const POST = withApiLogger(postHandler);
```

---

### 关键内容摘要

| 文件 | 要点 |
|------|------|
| `dingtalk.ts` | 提供 `sendDingtalkWorkMessage`（单条推送）和 `pushPendingDingtalkNotifs`（批量推送），token 模
</task_result>
```

404:   /// 提及类型：assign=派任务 discuss=拉讨论
405:   kind              String   @db.VarChar(16)
406:   /// 原始文本（含 @姓名）
407:   text              String   @db.Text
408:   /// 创建时间（北京时间）
409:   createdAt         DateTime @default(now())
410:   /// 钉钉推送时间（北京时间；NULL 表示未推送）
411:   dingtalkPushedAt  DateTime?
412: 
413:   node              Node     @relation(fields: [nodeId], references: [id])
414: 
415:   @@index([nodeId])
416:   @@index([mentionedUserId])
417:   @@map("mention_events")
418: }
419:

421: // 通知

427:   id                  Int      @id @default(autoincrement())

429:   recipientId         Int
430:   /// 触发者用户 ID（系统通知为 NULL）

434:   /// 通知标题

495:

135: ## [2026-05-19] 修复直属上级设置后申请关注提示"没有上级"
136: 
137: ### 根因
138: `users.managerId`（管理员面板写入）与 `OrgRelation` 表（`getAllSolidAncestors` 读取）是两套独立数据，设置 managerId 时未同步 OrgRelation，导致关注申请弹窗找不到上级。
139: 
140: ### 修复
141: - B-08-001 `POST /api/admin/users`：创建用户时若指定 managerId，同步创建 `OrgRelation(solid)` 记录
142: - B-08-002 `PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]`：修改 managerId 时，先删除该用户现有实线上级关系，再按新值创建
143: - B-05-002 `RequestFollowDialog`：ancestors 合并 OrgRelation + User.managerId 两路来源，去重后展示，作为兜底防止历史数据不一致
144: - B-05-003 `ShareDialog`：同上，修复分享弹窗"没有上级"问题
145: - B-08-003 `AdminUsersPage`：保存用户后调用 `refreshWorkspace()`，使当前会话的 `relations` 立即更新
146: 
147: ### 新增
148: - `getAllAncestorsByManagerId(userId, users)` 工具函数（`src/lib/org.ts`）：通过 User.managerId 链向上追溯所有上级
149: 
150: ## [2026-05-19] 修复下属在 TeamPage 不可见 & 同意关注 UX 反馈
151: 
152: ### 根因
153: `isManager` / `getAllSolidDescendants` 仅读 OrgRelation，历史数据中 OrgRelation 可能缺失，导致：
154: 1. AppShell "团队视图" 导航项对实际管理者隐藏
155: 2. TeamPage `allMembers` 为空，下属任务不可见
156: 3. MindMapPage "派任务" 按钮对实际管理者隐藏
157: 4. InboxPage 同意关注请求时无任何 toast 反馈（成功/失败）
158: 
159: ### 修复
160: - B-03-001 `src/lib/org.ts`：新增 `getAllDescendantsByManagerId(userId, users)` 函数，沿 User.managerId 链向下 BFS 遍历所有下属
161: - B-03-001 `src/pages/TeamPage.tsx`：`allMembers` useMemo 合并 `getAllSolidDescendants`（OrgRelation） + `getAllDescendantsByManagerId`（managerId链），去重后展示；isDirect 同步考虑 managerId 直属关系
162: - B-03-001 `src/components/AppShell.tsx`：`userIsManager` 增加 `users.some(u => u.managerId === currentUserId)` 兜底；useStore 解构增加 `users`
163: - B-03-001 `src/pages/MindMapPage.tsx`：`userIsManager` 增加相同 managerId 兜底
164: - B-05-004 `src/pages/InboxPage.tsx`：`decideFollow` 增加 toast 导入；pair 成功时 `toast.success("已同意关注，副本已添加到你的导图")`；pair 为 null 时 `toast.success("已同意关注")` + `toast.info("未能在你的导图中创建副本（骨架节点不匹配）...")`
165: 
166: ## [2026-05-19] 修复关注审批副本创建失败 & TeamPage 下属任务不显示
167: 
168: ### 根因
169: `GET /api/workspace` 仅加载当前用户自有的 mindmaps/nodes（`ownerId = userId`）。上级审批关注申请时，下级节点（`target`）不在上级的 `nodes` 状态中，导致：
170: 1. `pairNodesForFollowGrant` 中 `target = undefined` → 返回 null → 无法创建副本，只能触发 toast.info 降级路径
171: 2. TeamPage `memberMapIds` 正确，但 store 中无下级节点数据，下属任务栏始终为空
172: 
173: ### 修复
174: - B-05-005 `src/app/api/workspace/route.ts`：`getHandler` 在加载自有数据后，额外收集跨用户节点 ID（FollowGrant.targetNodeId 其中 granteeId=userId 含 pending 状态；Assignment.resultNodeId 其中 assignerId=userId），查询其所属导图（排除自有），并发加载 extraMindmaps / extraNodes / extraRelationships / extraLogs，以 id 去重合并后写入 snapshot。日志新增额外加载数量统计。
175: 
176: ## [2026-05-19] 修复派任务界面无法带出下属
177: 
178: ### 根因
179: `AssignDialog` 的 `directReportIds` 和 `allReportIds` 仅调用 `getDirectReports` / `getAllAssignTargets`（均只读 OrgRelation），未走 `User.managerId` 兜底链路，历史数据中 OrgRelation 缺失时下属列表为空。
180: 
181: ### 修复
182: - B-05-006 `src/features/assignment/AssignDialog.tsx`：引入 `getAllDescendantsByManagerId`；`directReportIds` useMemo 合并 OrgRelation 直接下属 + `users.filter(u => u.managerId === currentUserId)`；`allReportIds` useMemo 合并 `getAllAssignTargets` + `getAllDescendantsByManagerId`，两路均去重，与 TeamPage / AppShell 修复保持一致。
183: 
184: ## [2026-05-19] 修复"派出"按钮点击无效
185: 
186: ### 根因
187: `mindmapForAssigneeBucket` 需要在 `mindmaps` 中找到 `ownerId === assigneeId` 的导图，但 `GET /api/workspace` 只加载当前用户自有导图，以及已有 FollowGrant/Assignment 关系的跨用户导图。首次派任务时，下属既没有 FollowGrant 也没有 Assignment，其 mindmap 和骨架节点不在 store 中，导致所有 assignee 被跳过，`newAssignments.length === 0`，`toast.error` 或按钮因 title 为空而 disabled。
188: 
189: ### 修复
190: - B-05-007 `src/app/api/workspace/route.ts`：在跨用户加载之后新增"下属骨架数据加载"块：通过 `users` 数组 BFS 遍历 `User.managerId` 链，找到所有直/间接下属 ID；加载其全部 mindmap；再加载这些 mindmap 中的 `nodeType = "skeleton"` 节点（轻量）；三路合并到 `mergedMindmaps` / `mergedNodes`（以 id 去重，自有数据优先）。日志新增下属骨架加载数量统计。
191: 
192: ### 影响
193: - 上级加载工作区后，下级节点已在 `nodes` 状态中，`pairNodesForFollowGrant` 可正确执行，审批关注后副本创建成功
194: - TeamPage 下属任务数据正常显示
195: - PUT /api/workspace 写权限不变（跨用户节点无 `ownerId=userId` 匹配，不会被误写）
196: - 前端 `canRead` 权限过滤不变，额外数据不越权暴露
197: 
198: ## [2026-05-19] 修复派出无匹配骨架节点 & 修复 PUT 数据污染
199: 
200: ### 根因 B-05-008
201: 下属若从未登录，其名下没有年度导图和骨架节点。管理者加载工作区后 `subMindmaps` 为空，`mindmapForAssigneeBucket` 找不到骨架节点，所有 assignee 被跳过，`toast.error("所有目标人都没有匹配的骨架节点...")`。
202: 
203: ### 修复 B-05-008
204: - `GET /api/workspace` 加载 `subMindmaps` 后，遍历 `subordinateIds`：对没有当前年度 `useAnnualTemplate` 导图的下属代为创建年度导图、12 个月骨架节点、4 个季度骨架节点（逻辑与当前用户自动初始化一致，`createdBy = subId`）。随后的 `subSkeletonNodes` 查询即可取到新建的骨架节点。
205: 
206: ### 根因 B-05-009
207: `PUT /api/workspace` 的节点软删除和联系线删除两步缺少所有权约束：
208: - 节点软删除：`snapMindmapIds` 包含下属导图 ID，下属的 task 节点（非 skeleton）不在快照中，也不在 `snapNodeIds` 里，每次管理者保存工作区都会被误标 `isDeleted`，造成下属数据损坏。
209: - 联系线删除：`snapMindmapIds` 含下属导图 ID，下属联系线不在 `snapRelIds` 中，会被 `deleteMany` 误删。
210: 
211: ### 修复 B-05-009
212: - 节点软删除 `where` 新增 `mindmap: { ownerId: userId }` 约束（Prisma 关联字段过滤），确保只软删自己导图中的节点。
213: - 联系线删除 `where` 新增 `createdBy: userId` 约束（`Relationship` 无 `mindmap` 关联，改用创建者字段过滤），只删自己创建的联系线。
214: - TypeScript 零错误。

(End of file - total 214 lines)
</content>
```

**Title:** home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/lib/notify.ts

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/lib/notify.ts"

```

**Output:**
```
<path>/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/src/lib/notify.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: import type {
2:   Assignment,
3:   FollowGrant,
4:   MindMap,
5:   Node,
6:   NodeShare,
7:   OrgRelation,
8:   UserId,
9: } from "@/types";
10: import { ownerOfNode } from "./permission";
11: 
12: /**
13:  * 当某个任务节点 (status / progress / 内容) 发生变更时，需要被同步通知的人。
14:  * 包含：
15:  *  - 派任务人（accepted Assignment 的 assignerId）
16:  *  - 关注人（granted FollowGrant 的 granteeId，scope=single_task 或 subtree）
17:  *  - 主动分享对象（NodeShare.audienceId，未撤销）
18:  *  - 该节点 owner 的实线上级中"在派任务链路上"的中间层（沿用既有可见性规则；这里简化只取 assigner）
19:  *
20:  * 排除：变更发起人自己。
21:  */
22: export function collectTaskUpdateRecipients(args: {
23:   node: Node;
24:   actorId: UserId;
25:   mindmaps: MindMap[];
26:   nodes: Node[];
27:   assignments: Assignment[];
28:   follows: FollowGrant[];
29:   shares: NodeShare[];
30:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars
31:   relations: OrgRelation[];
32: }): UserId[] {
33:   const { node, actorId, mindmaps, nodes, assignments, follows, shares } = args;
34: 
35:   const recipients = new Set<UserId>();
36: 
37:   const owner = ownerOfNode(node, mindmaps);
38: 
39:   // 1. 派任务人：node 是某 accepted Assignment 的 resultNodeId，或 node 是其后代
40:   const ancestorIds = new Set<string>();
41:   ancestorIds.add(node.id);
42:   let cursor: string | undefined = node.parentId;
43:   while (cursor) {
44:     ancestorIds.add(cursor);
45:     const p = nodes.find((n) => n.id === cursor);
46:     cursor = p?.parentId;
47:   }
48:   for (const a of assignments) {
49:     if (!a.resultNodeId) continue;
50:     if (a.state !== "accepted" && a.state !== "adjusted") continue;
51:     if (ancestorIds.has(a.resultNodeId)) {
52:       recipients.add(a.assignerId);
53:     }
54:   }
55: 
56:   // 2. 关注人
57:   for (const f of follows) {
58:     if (f.state !== "granted") continue;
59:     if (f.scope === "single_task" && f.targetNodeId === node.id) {
60:       recipients.add(f.granteeId);
61:     } else if (f.scope === "subtree" && ancestorIds.has(f.targetNodeId)) {
62:       recipients.add(f.granteeId);
63:     }
64:   }
65: 
66:   // 3. 主动分享
67:   for (const s of shares) {
68:     if (s.revokedAt) continue;
69:     if (s.nodeId === node.id) {
70:       recipients.add(s.audienceId);
71:     }
72:   }
73: 
74:   // 排除自己 + 节点所有者（owner 本身就是改动发起人时不需通知；如果 actor 是别人，owner 也不需被通知自己的节点）
75:   recipients.delete(actorId);
76:   if (owner) recipients.delete(owner);
77: 
78:   return Array.from(recipients);
79: }

(End of file - total 79 lines)
</content>
```
