```
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: # M-07 通知中心
2: 
3: **状态：ACTIVE**
4: 
5: ## 概述
6: 
7: 接收系统内各类事件通知（任务派发、关注授权、汇报提交、@ 提及、日历同步等），支持按类型筛选、标记已读。
8: 
9: ## 数据模型
10: 
11: ### app_notifications 表
12: 
13: | 字段 | 说明 |
14: |------|------|
15: | id | INT 自增主键 |
16: | recipientId | 接收者用户 ID |
17: | actorId | 触发者用户 ID（可为空） |
18: | kind | 通知类型（见下） |
19: | title | 标题 |
20: | body | 正文 |
21: | refNodeId / refAssignmentId / refFollowGrantId / refReportId | 关联资源 ID |
22: | readAt | 读取时间（NULL = 未读） |
23: | dingtalkPushedAt | 钉钉推送时间 |
24: 
25: **通知类型（kind）：**
26: 
27: | 值 | 说明 |
28: |----|------|
29: | assignment_received | 收到新任务派发 |
30: | assignment_negotiating | 下级发起协商 |
31: | assignment_accepted | 下级接受任务 |
32: | assignment_rejected | 下级拒绝任务 |
33: | follow_requested | 收到节点关注申请 |
34: | follow_approved | 关注申请被批准 |
35: | follow_rejected | 关注申请被拒绝 |
36: | report_submitted | 收到汇报提交 |
37: | report_shared | 汇报抄送通知 |
38: | mention | @ 提及 |
39: | calendar_reminder | 日历截止提醒 |
40: 
41: ## API 接口
42: 
43: 通过 `GET/PUT /api/workspace`（M-02）整体同步。
44: 
45: ## 业务逻辑
46: 
47: - 所有业务操作（派任务、提交汇报等）均在 `StoreProvider` 内直接创建通知记录
48: - 点击通知可跳转至对应页面，跳转规则如下：
49:   - `follow_request_received` / `assignment_received` / `assignment_negotiating` / `follow_granted` / `follow_denied` → `/inbox`
50:   - `assignment_accepted` / `assignment_adjusted`（当前用户为派出方）→ `/team?member=<assigneeId>`
51:   - `assignment_accepted` / `assignment_adjusted`（当前用户为被派方）→ `/mindmap?node=<id>`
52:   - `node_shared` → `/team?member=<actorId>`
53:   - `task_status_changed` / `task_progress_updated` / `task_blocked` → `/team?member=<actorId>`（下级任务动态通知，上级以旁观者视角查看，避免误入下级导图）
54:   - `mentioned_assign` / `mentioned_discuss` / `calendar_synced` / `calendar_completion` → `/mindmap?node=<id>`
55: - 跳转 `/team` 时携带 `?member=<userId>` 查询参数，TeamPage 消费后自动切换到对应成员 tab，并立即调用 `router.replace("/team")` 清除参数（与 MindMapPage 处理 `?node=` 的模式一致）
56: 
57: ## 前端组件
58: 
59: - `src/pages/NotificationsPage.tsx`：通知列表，筛选/已读/跳转
60: 
61: ## 变更记录
62: 
63: | 日期 | 编号 | 变更内容 | 原始需求 |
64: |------|------|----------|----------|
```

现在我已有足够信息，整理全面报告如下。

---

## 探索结果报告

---

### 一、项目整体业务功能概述

这是一个**企业内部工作管理平台**，核心以"思维导图"为载体组织任务，配合完整的组织架构与协作工作流。主要功能模块如下：

| 模块 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| **M-01 认证** | 工号+密码登录（bcrypt+JWT），首次登录强制重置密码，IP 限流防暴力破解 |
| **M-02 工作区** | `GET/PUT /api/workspace` 全量快照同步，含跨用户节点（下属骨架、关注节点）的聚合加载 |
| **M-03 组织** | 部门树 + 实线/虚线汇报关系（OrgRelation）+ User.managerId 双路径 |
| **M-04 思维导图** | 思维导图创建与节点管理，节点可升级为任务，含附件、联系线、浮动主题等 |
| **M-05 任务派发与协作** | 上级向下级派任务（Assignment），下级可接受/协商/拒绝；关注授权（FollowGrant）申请查看上级节点；节点分享（NodeShare）；@ 提及（MentionEvent）触发通知 |
| **M-06 工作汇报** | 周报/月报/季报（WorkReport），提交给直属上级并抄送同事 |
| **M-07 通知中心** | 应用内通知（AppNotification）+ 钉钉推送；支持按类型筛选、标记已读、跳转关联页面 |
| **M-08 用户管理** | 管理员创建/编辑/禁用用户，设置直接上级 |
| **M-09 部门管理** | 部门树的增删改，有成员时拒绝删除 |

**API 路由全览：**

```
POST   /api/auth/login
POST   /api/auth/reset-password
GET    /api/org
PUT    /api/org
GET    /api/workspace
PUT    /api/workspace
POST   /api/workspace/reset
GET    /api/admin/users
POST   /api/admin/users
PATCH  /api/admin/users/[id]
DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]
GET    /api/admin/departments
POST   /api/admin/departments
PATCH  /api/admin/departments/[id]
DELETE /api/admin/departments/[id]
```

> 注：`workspaceApi.ts` 中还预留了尚未实现的接口调用：`/api/auth/dingtalk/exchange`（钉钉免登）、`/api/integrations/dingtalk/enqueue`（工作通知入队）、`/api/integrations/dingtalk/calendar/push`（日历推送）。

---

### 二、涉及"消息通知"/"发送消息"的业务场景

共有以下触发通知的业务场景（对应 `AppNotification.kind`）：

| 场景 | kind | 触发时机 | 通知对象 | 是否有钉钉推送 |
|------|------|---------|---------|--------------|
| 收到任务派发 | `assignment_received` | 上级发起派任务 | 被派下级 | 待接入 |
| 下级发起协商 | `assignment_negotiating` | 下级请求调整 | 派单上级 | 待接入 |
| 下级接受任务 | `assignment_accepted` | 下级点击接受 | 派单上级 | 待接入 |
| 下级拒绝任务 | `assignment_rejected` | 下级点击拒绝 | 派单上级 | 待接入 |
| 收到关注申请 | `follow_requested` | 下级申请查看节点 | 被申请上级 | 待接入 |
| 关注申请被批准 | `follow_approved` | 上级同意 | 申请下级 | 待接入 |
| 关注申请被拒绝 | `follow_rejected` | 上级拒绝 | 申请下级 | 待接入 |
| 收到汇报提交 | `report_submitted` | 下级提交工作汇报 | 直属上级 | 待接入 |
| 汇报抄送 | `report_shared` | 提交汇报时 CC | 被抄送同事 | 待接入 |
| @ 提及 | `mention` | 评论/描述中 @某人 | 被提及用户 | **已 mock**（通过 `dingtalkBound` 字段判断） |
| 日历截止提醒 | `calendar_reminder` | 日历同步时 | 节点所有者 | 待接入 |
| 任务状态变更 | `task_status_changed` | 节点 status 变更 | 派任务人+关注人+分享对象 | 待接入 |
| 任务进度更新 | `task_progress_updated` | progressPct 变更 | 同上 | 待接入 |
| 任务阻塞 | `task_blocked` | 标记阻塞 | 同上 | 待接入 |
| 节点分享 | `node_shared` | NodeShare 创建 | 接收者 | 待接入 |

通知接收对象的收集逻辑集中在 `src/lib/notify.ts`（`collectTaskUpdateRecipients`），综合考虑：派任务链路上的 assigner、已 granted 的 FollowGrant 关注人、未撤销的 NodeShare 分享对象。

---

### 三、现有用户模型（User）关键字段

```
id              INT 自增主键
employeeNo      工号（唯一）
name            姓名
email           邮箱（唯一）
passwordHash    密码哈希
avatar          头像
departmentId    所属部门
jobTitle        岗位职称
status          active / disabled
isAdmin         是否管理员
dingtalkBound   是否绑定钉钉  ← 已有钉钉字段
connectedCalendars  已连接日历（JSON 数组）
managerId       直接上级用户 ID
mustResetPassword   是否需要首次重置密码
```

**关键结论：**
- ✅ 有 **邮箱**（`email`）字段，且唯一
- ❌ **无手机号**字段（schema 中不存在 `phone` / `mobile` 字段）
- ✅ 已有 **`dingtalkBound`** 布尔字段，用于判断是否推送钉钉消息

---

### 四、环境变量中的钉钉相关配置

`.env.example` 中已预留钉钉配置段（注释状态，**尚未启用**）：

```bash
# 钉钉集成（可选，M3 钉钉通知/日历模块）
# DINGTALK_APP_KEY=your_app_key
# DINGTALK_APP_SECRET=your_app_secret
# DINGTALK_AGENT_ID=your_agent_id
```

**结论：** 钉钉集成变量已在 `.env.example` 中规划，但三个变量均处于注释状态，服务端相关 API 路由（`/api/integrations/dingtalk/*`、`/api/auth/dingtalk/exchange`）在 `workspaceApi.ts` 中已有前端调用占位，但对应的 Route Handler 文件**尚未创建**。

---

```
1: /**
2:  * GET  /api/admin/users  — 查询用户列表（仅管理员）
3:  * POST /api/admin/users  — 创建用户，初始密码固定为 123456（仅管理员）
4:  *
5:  * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
6:  * 规范 4-2：操作前校验 isAdmin
7:  * 规范 4-3：getAuth 鉴权
8:  */
9: 
10: import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
11: import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
12: import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
13: import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
14: import { hashPassword } from "@/lib/auth";
15: import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";
16: 
17: /** 初始密码（管理员创建用户时使用，用户首次登录后应自行修改） */
18: const INITIAL_PASSWORD = "123456";
19: 
20: // ── 工具：序列化用户行 ──────────────────────────────────────────
21: function serializeUser(u: {
22:   id: number;
23:   employeeNo: string;
24:   name: string;
25:   email: string;
26:   avatar: string | null;
27:   departmentId: number;
28:   jobTitle: string;
29:   status: string;
30:   isAdmin: boolean;
31:   dingtalkBound: boolean;
32:   managerId: number | null;
33:   mustResetPassword: boolean;
34: }) {
35:   return {
36:     id: String(u.id),
37:     employeeNo: u.employeeNo,
38:     name: u.name,
39:     email: u.email,
40:     avatar: u.avatar ?? undefined,
41:     departmentId: String(u.departmentId),
42:     jobTitle: u.jobTitle,
43:     status: u.status,
44:     isAdmin: u.isAdmin,
45:     dingtalkBound: u.dingtalkBound,
46:     managerId: u.managerId ? String(u.managerId) : undefined,
47:     mustResetPassword: u.mustResetPassword,
48:   };
49: }
50: 
51: // ── GET ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
52: async function getHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
53:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
54: 
55:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
56:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
57:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可访问" }, { status: 403 });
58:   }
59: 
60:   const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
61:     orderBy: { id: "asc" },
62:     select: {
63:       id: true,
64:       employeeNo: true,
65:       name: true,
66:       email: true,
67:       avatar: true,
68:       departmentId: true,
69:       jobTitle: true,
70:       status: true,
71:       isAdmin: true,
72:       dingtalkBound: true,
73:       managerId: true,
74:       mustResetPassword: true,
75:     },
76:   });
77: 
78:   return NextResponse.json({ users: users.map(serializeUser) });
79: }
80: 
81: // ── POST ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
82: async function postHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
83:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
84: 
85:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
86:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
87:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
88:   }
89: 
90:   const body = (await req.json()) as {
91:     employeeNo?: string;
92:     name?: string;
93:     email?: string;
94:     departmentId?: string;
95:     jobTitle?: string;
96:     avatar?: string;
97:     managerId?: string;
98:   };
99: 
100:   const { employeeNo, name, email, departmentId, jobTitle, avatar, managerId } = body;
101: 
102:   if (!employeeNo?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
103:   if (!name?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "姓名不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
104:   if (!departmentId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
105:   if (!jobTitle?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "职位不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
106: 
107:   // 工号唯一性校验
108:   const existing = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { employeeNo: employeeNo.trim() } });
109:   if (existing) {
110:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号已存在" }, { status: 409 });
111:   }
112: 
113:   // 部门存在性校验（规范 4-2：后端独立鉴权，不信任前端传值）
114:   const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(departmentId) } });
115:   if (!dept) {
116:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
117:   }
118: 
119:   // 直接上级存在性校验（如果指定）
120:   let managerDbId: number | null = null;
121:   if (managerId) {
122:     managerDbId = parseInt(managerId);
123:     if (isNaN(managerDbId)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
124:     const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: managerDbId } });
125:     if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
126:   }
127: 
128:   const passwordHash = await hashPassword(INITIAL_PASSWORD);
129: 
130:   const created = await prisma.user.create({
131:     data: {
132:       employeeNo: employeeNo.trim(),
133:       name: name.trim(),
134:       email: email?.trim() || `${employeeNo.trim()}@company.local`,
135:       avatar: avatar?.trim() || null,
136:       departmentId: parseInt(departmentId),
137:       jobTitle: jobTitle.trim(),
138:       status: "active",
139:       passwordHash,
140:       isAdmin: false,
141:       managerId: managerDbId,
142:       mustResetPassword: true,
143:     },
144:     select: {
145:       id: true,
146:       employeeNo: true,
147:       name: true,
148:       email: true,
149:       avatar: true,
150:       departmentId: true,
151:       jobTitle: true,
152:       status: true,
153:       isAdmin: true,
154:       dingtalkBound: true,
155:       managerId: true,
156:       mustResetPassword: true,
157:     },
158:   });
159: 
160:   // 同步 OrgRelation：若设置了直属上级，创建实线汇报关系
161:   if (managerDbId) {
162:     const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
163:     await prisma.orgRelation.create({
164:       data: {
165:         subordinateId: created.id,
166:         managerId: managerDbId,
167:         relationType: "solid",
168:         effectiveFrom: today,
169:         effectiveTo: null,
170:       },
171:     });
172:     logger.info(
173:       { user: userId },
174:       `同步 OrgRelation：新用户 ${created.id} → 上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
175:     );
176:   }
177: 
178:   logger.info(
179:     { user: userId },
180:     `管理员创建用户：${created.employeeNo} ${created.name}`,
181:   );
182: 
183:   return NextResponse.json({ user: serializeUser(created) }, { status: 201 });
184: }
185: 
186: export const GET = withApiLogger(getHandler);
187: export const POST = withApiLogger(postHandler);

(End of file - total 187 lines)
```

```
1: /**
2:  * PATCH  /api/admin/users/[id]  — 更新用户信息（仅管理员）
3:  * DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]  — 禁用用户（软删除，仅管理员）
4:  *
5:  * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
6:  * 规范 4-2：操作前校验 isAdmin，且禁止管理员禁用自身
7:  */
8: 
9: import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
10: import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
11: import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
12: import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
13: import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";
14: 
15: // ── PATCH ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
16: async function patchHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
17:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
18: 
19:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
20:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
21:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
22:   }
23: 
24:   const targetId = parseInt((ctx?.params as Record<string, string>)?.id ?? "");
25:   if (isNaN(targetId)) {
26:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
27:   }
28: 
29:   const target = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: targetId } });
30:   if (!target) {
31:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 });
32:   }
33: 
34:   const body = (await req.json()) as {
35:     name?: string;
36:     email?: string;
37:     avatar?: string;
38:     departmentId?: string;
39:     jobTitle?: string;
40:     status?: string;
41:     isAdmin?: boolean;
42:     managerId?: string | null;
43:   };
44: 
45:   // 部门存在性校验
46:   if (body.departmentId !== undefined) {
47:     const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(body.departmentId) } });
48:     if (!dept) {
49:       return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
50:     }
51:   }
52: 
53:   // 直接上级存在性校验
54:   let managerDbId: number | null | undefined = undefined;
55:   if (body.managerId !== undefined) {
56:     if (body.managerId === null || body.managerId === "") {
57:       managerDbId = null;
58:     } else {
59:       const mid = parseInt(body.managerId);
60:       if (isNaN(mid)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
61:       if (mid === targetId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能将自己设为自己的上级" }, { status: 400 });
62:       const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: mid } });
63:       if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
64:       managerDbId = mid;
65:     }
66:   }
67: 
68:   // 禁止把自己的 isAdmin 去掉（防止锁死系统）
69:   if (targetId === userId && body.isAdmin === false) {
70:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能取消自己的管理员权限" }, { status: 400 });
71:   }
72: 
73:   const updated = await prisma.user.update({
74:     where: { id: targetId },
75:     data: {
76:       ...(body.name !== undefined && { name: body.name.trim() }),
77:       ...(body.email !== undefined && { email: body.email.trim() }),
78:       ...(body.avatar !== undefined && { avatar: body.avatar.trim() || null }),
79:       ...(body.departmentId !== undefined && { departmentId: parseInt(body.departmentId) }),
80:       ...(body.jobTitle !== undefined && { jobTitle: body.jobTitle.trim() }),
81:       ...(body.status !== undefined && { status: body.status }),
82:       ...(body.isAdmin !== undefined && { isAdmin: body.isAdmin }),
83:       ...(managerDbId !== undefined && { managerId: managerDbId }),
84:     },
85:     select: {
86:       id: true,
87:       employeeNo: true,
88:       name: true,
89:       email: true,
90:       avatar: true,
91:       departmentId: true,
92:       jobTitle: true,
93:       status: true,
94:       isAdmin: true,
95:       dingtalkBound: true,
96:       managerId: true,
97:       mustResetPassword: true,
98:     },
99:   });
100: 
101:   // 同步 OrgRelation：managerId 字段有变更时，重建实线汇报关系
102:   if (managerDbId !== undefined) {
103:     // 删除该用户现有的所有实线上级关系
104:     await prisma.orgRelation.deleteMany({
105:       where: { subordinateId: targetId, relationType: "solid" },
106:     });
107:     if (managerDbId !== null) {
108:       const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
109:       await prisma.orgRelation.create({
110:         data: {
111:           subordinateId: targetId,
112:           managerId: managerDbId,
113:           relationType: "solid",
114:           effectiveFrom: today,
115:           effectiveTo: null,
116:         },
117:       });
118:       logger.info(
119:         { user: userId },
120:         `同步 OrgRelation：用户 ${targetId} → 新上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
121:       );
122:     } else {
123:       logger.info(
124:         { user: userId },
125:         `同步 OrgRelation：清除用户 ${targetId} 的实线上级关系`,
126:       );
127:     }
128:   }
129: 
130:   logger.info({ user: userId }, `管理员更新用户 ${targetId}：${JSON.stringify(body)}`);
131: 
132:   return NextResponse.json({
133:     user: {
134:       id: String(updated.id),
135:       employeeNo: updated.employeeNo,
136:       name: updated.name,
137:       email: updated.email,
138:       avatar: updated.avatar ?? undefined,
139:       departmentId: String(updated.departmentId),
140:       jobTitle: updated.jobTitle,
141:       status: updated.status,
142:       isAdmin: updated.isAdmin,
143:       dingtalkBound: updated.dingtalkBound,
144:       managerId: updated.managerId ? String(updated.managerId) : undefined,
145:       mustResetPassword: updated.mustResetPassword,
146:     },
147:   });
148: }
149: 
150: // ── DELETE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
151: async function deleteHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
152:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
153: 
154:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
155:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
156:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
157:   }
158: 
159:   const targetId = parseInt((ctx?.params as Record<string, string>)?.id ?? "");
160:   if (isNaN(targetId)) {
161:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
162:   }
163: 
164:   // 禁止管理员删除自身
165:   if (targetId === userId) {
166:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能禁用自己的账号" }, { status: 400 });
167:   }
168: 
169:   const target = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: targetId } });
170:   if (!target) {
171:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 });
172:   }
173: 
174:   // 软删除：状态改为 disabled
175:   await prisma.user.update({
176:     where: { id: targetId },
177:     data: { status: "disabled" },
178:   });
179: 
180:   logger.info({ user: userId }, `管理员禁用用户 ${targetId}（${target.employeeNo} ${target.name}）`);
181: 
182:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true });
183: }
184: 
185: export const PATCH = withApiLogger(patchHandler);
186: export const DELETE = withApiLogger(deleteHandler);

(End of file - total 186 lines)
```

```
  Line 545:   "content": "## 为什么\n\n现有的通知中心（M-07）只支持应用内通知（AppNotification），用户必须主动打开系统才能查看消息。在实际企业场景中，任务派发、协商、审批、汇报等关键操作需要通过钉钉即时触达当事人，避免因遗漏通知导致工作延误。项目数据库已有 `dingtalkBound` 字段，`.env.example` 中也预留了钉钉 App 配置，本次迭代正式将钉钉通知能力从\"待接入\"状态推向完整实现。\n\n## 变更内容\n\n- **新增** 钉钉工作通知发送服务（封装钉钉 OpenAPI）\n- **新增** 钉钉通知队列 API（`/api/integrations/dingtalk/enqueue`），供内部服务调用\n- **新增** 用户绑定钉钉 userId 的字段（`User.dingtalkUserId`），用于调用钉钉发消息接口\n- **新增** 管理员在用户管理页面录入/维护员工的钉钉 userId\n- **修改** 所有触发 AppNotification 的业务场景，在创建站内通知的同时，异步向绑定了钉钉的用户推送钉钉工作通知\n- **修改** 环境变量说明，启用钉钉相关配置项\n\n涉及的通知场景（共 15 类，全部对齐）：\n\n| 场景 | kind |\n|------|------|\n| 收到任务派发 | `assignment_received` |\n| 下级发起协商 | `assignment_negotiating` |\n| 下级接受任务 | `assignment_accepted` |\n| 下级拒绝任务 | `assignment_rejected` |\n| 收到关注申请 | `follow_requested` |\n| 关注申请被批准 | `follow_approved` |\n| 关注申请被拒绝 | `follow_rejected` |\n| 收到汇报提交 | `report_submitted` |\n| 汇报抄送 | `report_shared` |\n| @ 提及 | `mention` |\n| 日历截止提醒 | `calendar_reminder` |\n| 任务状态变更 | `task_status_changed` |\n| 任务进度更新 | `task_progress_updated` |\n| 任务阻塞 | `task_blocked` |\n| 节点分享 | `node_shared` |\n\n## 功能 (Capabilities)\n\n### 新增功能\n\n- `dingtalk-service`: 封装钉钉 OpenAPI 的服务层，含获取 access_token、发送工作通知（sendWorkMessage）两个核心能力\n- `dingtalk-notification-dispatch`: 在所有触发站内通知的业务节点，额外向绑定了钉钉的用户发送钉钉工作通知的调度逻辑\n\n### 修改功能\n\n- `user-management`: 用户管理新增 `dingtalkUserId` 字段的录入与维护（管理员在用户编辑表单中填写）\n- `notification-center`: AppNotification 创建时同步触发钉钉推送，通知内容与站内消息保持一致\n\n## 影响\n\n- **数据库**：`User` 表新增 `dingtalkUserId VARCHAR(64)` 字段；需执行 `prisma migrate`\n- **环境变量**：启用 `DINGTALK_APP_KEY`、`DINGTALK_APP_SECRET`、`DINGTALK_AGENT_ID`\n- **新增文件**：`src/lib/dingtalk.ts`（钉钉服务）\n- **修改文件**：`src/lib/notify.ts`（所有 `createNotification` 调用点追加钉钉推送）、`prisma/schema.prisma`、`src/app/api/admin/users/[id]/route.ts`、对应的前端用户编辑表单\n- **依赖**：无需新增 npm 包，使用原生 `fetch` 调用钉钉 HTTP API\n"

  Line 674: **Title:** home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/design.md

  Line 679:   "content": "## 上下文\n\n项目已有完整的站内通知系统（M-07 AppNotification），所有通知均通过 `src/lib/notify.ts` 的 `createNotification()` 函数统一创建。钉钉推送在早期设计中已预留了 `User.dingtalkBound` 字段和 `.env.example` 配置项，但对应的实现层（钉钉 API 封装、发送调用）一直缺失。\n\n本次迭代在不改变现有站内通知逻辑的前提下，在 `createNotification()` 调用链末端追加钉钉异步推送，保持现有代码结构稳定。\n\n## 目标 / 非目标\n\n**目标：**\n- 封装钉钉企业内部应用工作通知 API（发消息接口）\n- 用户表新增 `dingtalkUserId` 字段，管理员可在用户编辑页录入\n- 所有 15 类通知场景在创建站内通知的同时，向已绑定钉钉的用户异步推送工作通知\n- 钉钉推送失败不影响主业务流程（静默降级）\n\n**非目标：**\n- 钉钉免登/OAuth 自动绑定（`dingtalkUserId` 由管理员手动维护，不做自动同步）\n- 钉钉机器人/群消息（只做工作通知，不做群聊机器人）\n- 通知模板的富卡片（Markdown 卡片）样式，本期只做纯文本\n- 消息送达回执/已读状态同步\n- 推送失败重试队列（后续迭代可扩展）\n\n## 决策\n\n### 决策 1：直接调用 vs 消息队列\n\n**选择**：直接在 `createNotification()` 末尾发起异步调用（fire-and-forget），不引入独立的消息队列服务。\n\n**理由**：项目当前体量小，没有独立的 Worker/Queue 基础设施，引入 Redis Queue 会显著增加运维复杂度。采用 `void dingtalkSend(...)` 的 fire-and-forget 模式可满足当前需求，后续如需重试/幂等可在 `dingtalk.ts` 内部扩展。\n\n**替代方案**：`/api/integrations/dingtalk/enqueue` 异步队列 API（`workspaceApi.ts` 中已有占位）—— 本期不实现，保持占位即可。\n\n### 决策 2：access_token 缓存策略\n\n**选择**：在 `src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 中以模块级变量缓存 access_token（含过期时间戳），在过期前 5 分钟主动刷新。\n\n**理由**：钉钉 access_token 有效期 7200 秒，每次发消息前都重新获取会浪费 API 调用次数。模块级缓存在 Next.js 的 Node.js 进程中是可靠的，适合单实例部署。\n\n**替代方案**：存 Redis / 数据库 —— 对单实例部署过度设计。\n\n### 决策 3：dingtalkUserId 的维护方式\n\n**选择**：管理员在用户编辑表单中手动填写 `dingtalkUserId`（钉钉用户的 unionId 或 userId）。\n\n**理由**：`dingtalkBound` 字段本来就是布尔值，说明最初设计就是手动绑定。自动 OAuth 绑定需要独立的钉钉免登流程，超出本次迭代范围。手动维护适合企业内部管理员操作，实现成本最低。\n\n**字段使用**：`dingtalkBound` 字段保留（兼容现有逻辑），新增 `dingtalkUserId STRING?`；推送时判断 `dingtalkUserId != null` 即推送（自动设置 `dingtalkBound = true`）。\n\n### 决策 4：通知内容格式\n\n**选择**：纯文本格式，消息内容复用站内通知的 `content` 字段文本，附加应用名前缀（如 `【工作平台】`）。\n\n**理由**：钉钉工作通知支持 text/markdown/OA 等多种消息类型，但本期聚焦于消息触达，不做富卡片设计，避免后期维护两套通知文案。\n\n### 决策 5：推送失败处理\n\n**选择**：`try/catch` 捕获所有钉钉 API 错误，仅记录 `logger.warn` 日志，不抛出异常，不影响主业务 HTTP 响应。\n\n**理由**：钉钉 API 属于外部依赖，网络抖动/配置错误不应导致站内操作失败。日志中可见失败信息，便于排查。\n\n## 风险 / 权衡\n\n| 风险 | 缓解措施 |\n|------|---------|\n| 钉钉 access_token 在多实例部署时各实例独立缓存，可能同时刷新 | 当前为单实例部署，可接受；后...

  Line 864:   "content": "## 新增需求\n\n### 需求:获取钉钉 access_token\n系统必须能够通过企业内部应用的 AppKey 和 AppSecret 向钉钉 OpenAPI 获取 access_token，并将其缓存在模块级变量中，在过期前 5 分钟自动刷新。当 `DINGTALK_APP_KEY` 或 `DINGTALK_APP_SECRET` 环境变量未配置时，系统必须直接返回 null 并跳过所有钉钉操作，不得抛出异常。\n\n#### 场景:配置完整时获取 token\n- **当** 环境变量 `DINGTALK_APP_KEY` 和 `DINGTALK_APP_SECRET` 均已配置，且缓存为空或已过期\n- **那么** 系统向 `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken` 发起请求并返回有效 token，缓存过期时间戳\n\n#### 场景:缓存有效时复用 token\n- **当** 缓存的 access_token 距离过期时间超过 5 分钟\n- **那么** 系统直接返回缓存 token，不发起网络请求\n\n#### 场景:环境变量未配置时跳过\n- **当** `DINGTALK_APP_KEY` 或 `DINGTALK_APP_SECRET` 任一为空\n- **那么** 系统返回 null，不发起任何网络请求，不抛出异常\n\n### 需求:发送钉钉工作通知\n系统必须提供 `sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId: string, content: string)` 函数，通过钉钉企业内部应用工作通知接口向指定用户发送纯文本消息。发送失败时必须记录 `logger.warn` 日志，禁止抛出异常影响调用方业务流程。\n\n#### 场景:成功发送工作通知\n- **当** access_token 有效，`dingtalkUserId` 非空，且钉钉 API 返回 `errcode=0`\n- **那么** 消息成功投递，函数正常返回\n\n#### 场景:发送失败静默降级\n- **当** 钉钉 API 返回非 0 errcode 或网络请求抛出异常\n- **那么** 系统记录 `logger.warn` 包含错误信息和 userId，函数正常返回不抛出异常\n\n#### 场景:DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 未配置时跳过\n- **当** 环境变量 `DINGTALK_AGENT_ID` 未配置\n- **那么** 函数直接返回不发起请求，不记录错误日志\n",

  Line 888:   "content": "## 新增需求\n\n### 需求:创建站内通知时同步触发钉钉推送\n系统在调用 `createNotification()` 创建 AppNotification 后，必须检查接收用户的 `dingtalkUserId` 字段。若该字段非空，则异步调用 `sendDingtalkWorkMessage()` 向该用户推送内容相同的钉钉工作通知。钉钉推送必须以 fire-and-forget 方式执行，禁止 await 阻塞主流程，禁止因推送失败而影响 HTTP 响应。\n\n#### 场景:绑定钉钉的用户收到通知\n- **当** 系统调用 `createNotification()` 且接收用户的 `dingtalkUserId` 非空\n- **那么** 系统在创建站内通知后，以 fire-and-forget 方式向该用户发送内容为 `【工作平台】${notification.content}` 的钉钉工作通知\n\n#### 场景:未绑定钉钉的用户收到通知\n- **当** 系统调用 `createNotification()` 且接收用户的 `dingtalkUserId` 为 null 或空字符串\n- **那么** 系统只创建站内通知，不发起任何钉钉 API 调用\n\n#### 场景:钉钉推送失败不影响站内通知\n- **当** 钉钉推送调用抛出异常或返回错误\n- **那么** 站内通知已正常创建，API 响应正常返回，仅记录 warn 日志\n\n### 需求:所有 15 类通知场景均触发钉钉推送\n系统中所有触发站内通知的业务场景（`assignment_received`、`assignment_negotiating`、`assignment_accepted`、`assignment_rejected`、`follow_requested`、`follow_approved`、`follow_rejected`、`report_submitted`、`report_shared`、`mention`、`calendar_reminder`、`task_status_changed`、`task_progress_updated`、`task_blocked`、`node_shared`）必须均通过 `createNotification()` 统一入口触发钉钉推送，禁止各业务场景单独处理钉钉推送逻辑。\n\n#### 场景:任务派发触发钉钉通知\n- **当** 上级通过系统派发任务给下级，系统创建 `assignment_received` 类型的站内通知\n- **那么** 若被派发下级的 `dingtalkUserId` 非空，系统向其发送钉钉工作通知\n\n#### 场景:工作汇报提交触发钉钉通知\n- **当** 下级提交工作汇报，系统创建 `report_submitted` 类型的站内通知给直属上级\n- **那么** 若直属上级的 `dingtalkUserId` 非空，系统向其发送钉钉工作通知\n",
```

```
18: import { getApiToken } from "@/lib/api/workspaceApi";
19: import { useStore } from "@/store/StoreProvider";
20: import { UserPlus, Pencil, Ban, CheckCircle2 } from "lucide-react";
21: 
22: interface AdminUser {
23:   id: string;
24:   employeeNo: string;
25:   name: string;
26:   email: string;
27:   avatar?: string;
28:   departmentId: string;
29:   jobTitle: string;
30:   status: string;
31:   isAdmin: boolean;
32:   managerId?: string;
33: }
34: 
35: interface Dept {
36:   id: string;
37:   name: string;
38:   parentId?: string;
39: }
40: 
41: function authHeaders() {
42:   return { "Content-Type": "application/json", Authorization: `Bearer ${getApiToken()}` };
43: }
44: 
45: export default function AdminUsersPage() {
46:   const router = useRouter();
47:   const { currentUser, refreshWorkspace } = useStore();
48: 
49:   const [users, setUsers] = useState<AdminUser[]>([]);
50:   const [depts, setDepts] = useState<Dept[]>([]);
51:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
52: 
53:   // 新建/编辑对话框
54:   const [showForm, setShowForm] = useState(false);
55:   const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);
56:   const [form, setForm] = useState({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "" });
57:   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
58: 
59:   // 禁用确认
60:   const [disableTarget, setDisableTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);
61: 
62:   // 权限检查
63:   useEffect(() => {
64:     if (currentUser && !currentUser.isAdmin) {
65:       router.replace("/mindmap");
66:     }
67:   }, [currentUser, router]);
68: 
69:   const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
70:     setLoading(true);
71:     try {
72:       const [uRes, dRes] = await Promise.all([
73:         fetch("/api/admin/users", { headers: authHeaders() }),
74:         fetch("/api/admin/departments", { headers: authHeaders() }),
75:       ]);
76:       const uJson = await uRes.json() as { users?: AdminUser[]; error?: string };
77:       const dJson = await dRes.json() as { departments?: Dept[]; error?: string };
78:       if (!uRes.ok) throw new Error(uJson.error ?? "加载用户失败");
79:       if (!dRes.ok) throw new Error(dJson.error ?? "加载部门失败");
80:       setUsers(uJson.users ?? []);
81:       setDepts(dJson.departments ?? []);
82:     } catch (e) {
83:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
84:     } finally {
85:       setLoading(false);
86:     }
87:   }, []);
88: 
89:   useEffect(() => { void fetchData(); }, [fetchData]);
90: 
91:   function openCreate() {
92:     setEditTarget(null);
93:     setForm({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: depts[0]?.id ?? "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "" });
94:     setShowForm(true);
95:   }
96: 
97:   function openEdit(u: AdminUser) {
98:     setEditTarget(u);
99:     setForm({ employeeNo: u.employeeNo, name: u.name, email: u.email, avatar: u.avatar ?? "", departmentId: u.departmentId, jobTitle: u.jobTitle, managerId: u.managerId ?? "" });
100:     setShowForm(true);
101:   }
102: 
103:   async function handleSave() {
104:     if (!form.name.trim()) { toast.error("姓名不能为空"); return; }
105:     if (!form.departmentId) { toast.error("请选择部门"); return; }
106:     if (!form.jobTitle.trim()) { toast.error("职位不能为空"); return; }
107:     if (!editTarget && !form.employeeNo.trim()) { toast.error("工号不能为空"); return; }
108: 
109:     setSaving(true);
110:     try {
111:       if (editTarget) {
112:         const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${editTarget.id}`, {
113:           method: "PATCH",
114:           headers: authHeaders(),
115:           body: JSON.stringify({
116:             name: form.name,
117:             email: form.email,
118:             avatar: form.avatar,
119:             departmentId: form.departmentId,
120:             jobTitle: form.jobTitle,
121:             managerId: form.managerId || null,
122:           }),
123:         });
124:         const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
125:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "更新失败");
126:         setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === editTarget.id ? (d.user ?? u) : u));
127:         toast.success("用户信息已更新");
128:         // PATCH 总是包含 managerId，可能改变 OrgRelation，刷新全局 relations
129:         void refreshWorkspace();
130:       } else {
131:         const r = await fetch("/api/admin/users", {
132:           method: "POST",
133:           headers: authHeaders(),
134:           body: JSON.stringify({ ...form, managerId: form.managerId || undefined }),
135:         });
136:         const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
137:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "创建失败");
138:         setUsers(prev => [...prev, d.user!]);
139:         toast.success(`用户 ${form.name} 创建成功，初始密码：123456`);
140:         // 新用户若有直属上级，刷新全局 relations
141:         if (form.managerId) void refreshWorkspace();
142:       }
143:       setShowForm(false);
144:     } catch (e) {
145:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
146:     } finally {
147:       setSaving(false);
148:     }
149:   }
150: 
151:   async function handleDisable() {
152:     if (!disableTarget) return;
153:     try {
154:       const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${disableTarget.id}`, {
155:         method: "DELETE",
156:         headers: authHeaders(),
157:       });
158:       const d = await r.json() as { ok?: boolean; error?: string };
159:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
160:       setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === disableTarget.id ? { ...u, status: "disabled" } : u));
161:       toast.success(`用户 ${disableTarget.name} 已禁用`);
162:     } catch (e) {
163:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
164:     } finally {
165:       setDisableTarget(null);
166:     }
167:   }
168: 
169:   async function handleEnable(u: AdminUser) {
170:     try {
171:       const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}`, {
172:         method: "PATCH",
173:         headers: authHeaders(),
174:         body: JSON.stringify({ status: "active" }),
175:       });
176:       const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
177:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
178:       setUsers(prev => prev.map(usr => usr.id === u.id ? { ...usr, status: "active" } : usr));
179:       toast.success(`用户 ${u.name} 已启用`);
180:     } catch (e) {
181:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
182:     }
183:   }
184: 
185:   function deptName(id: string) {
186:     return depts.find(d => d.id === id)?.name ?? id;
187:   }
188: 
189:   return (
190:     <>
191:       <PageHeader
192:         title="用户管理"
193:         description="管理系统用户账号，新建用户初始密码为 123456"
194:         right={
195:           <Button onClick={openCreate} size="sm">
196:             <UserPlus className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
197:             新建用户
198:           </Button>
199:         }
200:       />
201: 
202:       <div className="flex-1 p-6 overflow-auto">
203:         {loading ? (
204:           <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">加载中…</div>
205:         ) : (
206:           <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-border overflow-hidden">
207:             <table className="w-full text-sm">
208:               <thead className="bg-slate-50 border-b border-border">
209:                 <tr>
210:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">工号</th>
211:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">姓名</th>
212:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">部门</th>
213:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">职位</th>
214:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">状态</th>
215:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">角色</th>
216:                   <th className="text-right px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">操作</th>
217:                 </tr>
218:               </thead>
219:               <tbody className="divide-y divide-border">
220:                 {users.map(u => (
221:                   <tr key={u.id} className="hover:bg-slate-50">
222:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{u.employeeNo}</td>
223:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 font-medium text-brand-ink">
224:                       {u.avatar ? <span className="mr-1">{u.avatar}</span> : null}
225:                       {u.name}
226:                     </td>
227:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{deptName(u.departmentId)}</td>
228:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{u.jobTitle}</td>
229:                     <td className="px-4 py-3">
230:                       <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${u.status === "active" ? "bg-green-50 text-green-700" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-500"}`}>
231:                         {u.status === "active" ? "正常" : "已禁用"}
232:                       </span>
233:                     </td>
234:                     <td className="px-4 py-3">
235:                       {u.isAdmin && (
236:                         <span className="inline-flex px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-orange-50 text-orange-700">管理员</span>
237:                       )}
238:                     </td>
239:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
240:                       <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">
241:                         <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => openEdit(u)} title="编辑">
242:                           <Pencil className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
243:                         </Button>
244:                         {u.status === "active" ? (
245:                           <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => setDisableTarget(u)} title="禁用" disabled={u.id === currentUser?.id}>
246:                             <Ban className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-destructive" />
247:                           </Button>
248:                         ) : (
249:                           <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => handleEnable(u)} title="启用">
250:                             <CheckCircle2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-600" />
251:                           </Button>
252:                         )}
253:                       </div>
254:                     </td>
255:                   </tr>
256:                 ))}
257:                 {users.length === 0 && (
258:                   <tr>
259:                     <td colSpan={7} className="px-4 py-10 text-center text-muted-foreground">
260:                       暂无用户，请点击右上角新建
261:                     </td>
262:                   </tr>
263:                 )}
264:               </tbody>
265:             </table>
266:           </div>
267:         )}
268:       </div>
269: 
270:       {/* 新建/编辑对话框 */}
271:       <Dialog open={showForm} onOpenChange={setShowForm}>
272:         <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
273:           <DialogHeader>
274:             <DialogTitle>{editTarget ? "编辑用户" : "新建用户"}</DialogTitle>
275:           </DialogHeader>
276:           <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
277:             {!editTarget && (
278:               <div className="space-y-1.5">
279:                 <Label>工号 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
280:                 <Input value={form.employeeNo} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, employeeNo: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 E011" />
281:               </div>
282:             )}
283:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
284:               <Label>姓名 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
285:               <Input value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, name: e.target.value }))} placeholder="真实姓名" />
286:             </div>
287:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
288:               <Label>邮箱</Label>
289:               <Input value={form.email} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, email: e.target.value }))} placeholder="可留空，自动生成" type="email" />
290:             </div>
291:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
292:               <Label>头像（emoji）</Label>
293:               <Input value={form.avatar} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, avatar: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 👤（可留空）" />
294:             </div>
295:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
296:               <Label>部门 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
297:               <select
298:                 className="w-full border border-input rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-background"
299:                 value={form.departmentId}
300:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, departmentId: e.target.value }))}
301:               >
302:                 <option value="">请选择部门</option>
303:                 {depts.map(d => (
304:                   <option key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name}</option>
305:                 ))}
306:               </select>
307:             </div>
308:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
309:               <Label>职位 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
310:               <Input value={form.jobTitle} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, jobTitle: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 产品经理" />
311:             </div>
312:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
313:               <Label>直接上级</Label>
314:               <select
315:                 className="w-full border border-input rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-background"
316:                 value={form.managerId}
317:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, managerId: e.target.value }))}
318:               >
319:                 <option value="">无上级</option>
320:                 {users
321:                   .filter(u => u.status === "active" && u.id !== editTarget?.id)
322:                   .map(u => (
323:                     <option key={u.id} value={u.id}>
324:                       {u.avatar ? `${u.avatar} ` : ""}{u.name}（{u.employeeNo}）
325:                     </option>
326:                   ))}
327:               </select>
328:             </div>
329:             {!editTarget && (
330:               <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-slate-50 rounded p-2">
331:                 新建用户初始密码为 <span className="font-mono font-semibold">123456</span>，请告知用户登录后及时修改。
332:               </p>
333:             )}
334:           </div>
335:           <DialogFooter>
336:             <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowForm(false)} disabled={saving}>取消</Button>
337:             <Button onClick={handleSave} disabled={saving}>{saving ? "保存中…" : "保存"}</Button>
338:           </DialogFooter>
339:         </DialogContent>
340:       </Dialog>
341: 
342:       {/* 禁用确认对话框 */}
343:       <ConfirmDialog
344:         open={!!disableTarget}
345:         title="禁用用户"
346:         description={`确定要禁用用户「${disableTarget?.name}」吗？禁用后该用户将无法登录。`}
347:         confirmLabel="禁用"
348:         destructive
349:         onConfirm={handleDisable}
350:         onCancel={() => setDisableTarget(null)}
351:       />
352:     </>
353:   );
354: }

(End of file - total 354 lines)
</content>
```

所有信息已收集完毕，下面是完整的汇总报告。

---

## 探索结果汇总

---

### 一、`.env` 中钉钉相关环境变量

文件路径：`/home/heyue/mindmap-docs-and-frontend/.env`

| 变量名 | 是否有值 | 说明 |
|---|---|---|
| `DINGTALK_APP_KEY` | ✅ 有值 | 钉钉企业内部应用的 AppKey |
| `DINGTALK_APP_SECRET` | ✅ 有值 | 钉钉企业内部应用的 AppSecret（敏感，隐藏） |
| `DINGTALK_AGENT_ID` | ✅ 有值 | 钉钉应用的 AgentId，用于工作通知接口 |

> 三个变量均已配置真实值（非注释状态），与 `.env.example` 中的注释占位不同，**当前 `.env` 已处于可用状态**。

---

### 二、`prisma/schema.prisma` — User model 完整字段列表

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 |
|---|---|---|
| `id` | `Int` (PK, 自增) | 主键 |
| `employeeNo` | `String` (unique, varchar 64) | 工号，全局唯一 |
| `name` | `String` (varchar 64) | 姓名 |
| `email` | `String` (unique, varchar 128) | 邮箱，全局唯一 |
| `passwordHash` | `String?` (varchar 128) | 密码哈希（bcrypt cost≥12），可为空 |
| `avatar` | `String?` (varchar 256) | 头像 emoji 或图片 URL |
| `departmentId` | `Int` | 所属部门 ID（外键 → Department） |
| `jobTitle` | `String` (varchar 64) | 岗位职称 |
| `status` | `String` (varchar 16, default "active") | 状态：`active`/`disabled` |
| `isAdmin` | `Boolean` (default false) | 是否为管理员 |
| `dingtalkBound` | `Boolean` (default false) | 是否绑定钉钉 |
| `connectedCalendars` | `Json?` | 已连接的日历（JSON 数组，如 `["mac","dingtalk","google"]`） |
| `managerId` | `Int?` | 直接上级用户 ID，NULL 表示无上级 |
| `mustResetPassword` | `Boolean` (default false) | 是否需要下次登录时重置密码 |
| `createdAt` | `DateTime` (default now()) | 创建时间（北京时间） |
| `updatedAt` | `DateTime` (@updatedAt) | 最后更新时间（北京时间） |

> **注意**：`dingtalkUserId` 字段**目前不存在**于 schema 中。根据 `openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/tasks.md`，这是本次钉钉通知迭代中计划新增的字段（任务 1.1），尚未执行迁移。

---

### 三、用户创建接口入参（`POST /api/admin/users`）

文件：`src/app/api/admin/users/route.ts`

| 字段 | 类型 | 必填 | 说明 |
|---|---|---|---|
| `employeeNo` | `string` | ✅ 必填 | 工号，不能为空，全局唯一校验 |
| `name` | `string` | ✅ 必填 | 姓名 |
| `email` | `string?` | 可选 | 邮箱，若留空自动生成 `{employeeNo}@company.local` |
| `departmentId` | `string` | ✅ 必填 | 部门 ID（字符串，后端 parseInt 转换），做存在性校验 |
| `jobTitle` | `string` | ✅ 必填 | 职位 |
| `avatar` | `string?` | 可选 | 头像 emoji |
| `managerId` | `string?` | 可选 | 直属上级用户 ID，做存在性校验；设置后自动同步创建 `OrgRelation` 实线汇报关系 |

> 其余字段由后端自动设定：`passwordHash`（初始密码 `123456` 的 bcrypt 哈希）、`status: "active"`、`isAdmin: false`、`mustResetPassword: true`。

---

### 四、用户编辑接口入参（`PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]`）

文件：`src/app/api/admin/users/[id]/route.ts`

| 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
|---|---|---|
| `name` | `string?` | 姓名 |
| `email` | `string?` | 邮箱 |
| `avatar` | `string?` | 头像 |
| `departmentId` | `string?` | 部门 ID，做存在性校验 |
| `jobTitle` | `string?` | 职位 |
| `status` | `string?` | 状态（如 `"active"`/`"disabled"`） |
| `isAdmin` | `boolean?` | 管理员权限，不能取消自己的管理员身份 |
| `managerId` | `string \| null?` | 直属上级 ID，空字符串或 null 表示清除；变更后自动重建 `OrgRelation` |

> `dingtalkUserId` 字段**当前接口尚未接受**，是本次迭代计划新增的（任务 4.1）。

---

### 五、前端用户创建/编辑表单字段

文件：`src/pages/admin/AdminUsersPage.tsx`

表单 state 结构：
```ts
{ employeeNo, name, email, avatar, departmentId, jobTitle, managerId }
```

| 表单字段 | 显示标签 | 必填 | 控件类型 | 备注 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `employeeNo` | 工号 * | ✅ | Input | **仅新建时显示**，编辑时不可修改工号 |
| `name` | 姓名 * | ✅ | Input | |
| `email` | 邮箱 | 可选 | Input (email) | 可留空，后端自动生成 |
| `avatar` | 头像（emoji） | 可选 | Input | 提示"如 👤（可留空）" |
| `departmentId` | 部门 * | ✅ | Select | 从 API 加载部门列表 |
| `jobTitle` | 职位 * | ✅ | Input | |
| `managerId` | 直接上级 | 可选 | Select | 从用户列表过滤 active 用户 |

> **当前表单没有 `dingtalkUserId` 输入框**，这是本次迭代计划新增的（任务 5.1）。

---

### 六、`src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 是否存在

**不存在**。`src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 文件目前**尚未创建**，这正是本次 `dingtalk-notification` 迭代中任务 2.1～2.3 计划新建的核心服务文件，将实现：
- `getDingtalkToken()` — 获取 + 缓存 access_token（模块级缓存，5 分钟提前刷新）
- `sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId, content)` — 发送工作通知，失败静默降级

---

### 七、项目中所有钉钉相关文件路径

**`src/` 目录下**（已实现的代码）：

| 文件 | 涉及钉钉的内容 |
|---|---|
| `src/lib/api/workspaceApi.ts` | 预留了 `/api/auth/dingtalk/exchange`（钉钉免登）、`/api/integrations/dingtalk/enqueue`（工作通知入队）、`/api/integrations/dingtalk/calendar/push`（日历推送）三个占位调用 |
| `src/lib/calendarSync.ts` | 日历同步，涉及 `dingtalk` provider |
| `src/lib/mentionEffects.ts` | `@提及` 场景，涉及 `dingtalkBound` 字段判断是否推送 |
| `src/pages/NotificationsPage.tsx` | 通知中心页面，涉及 `dingtalkPushedAt` 字段展示 |
| `src/types/index.ts` | 类型定义，含 `dingtalk` 相关类型 |
| `src/app/api/workspace/route.ts` | workspace 接口，返回含 `dingtalkBound` 的用户信息 |
| `src/app/api/admin/users/route.ts` | GET/POST 用户管理，序列化 `dingtalkBound` |
| `src/app/api/admin/users/[id]/route.ts` | PATCH/DELETE 用户，序列化 `dingtalkBound` |
| `src/mock/org.ts` | mock 数据，含 `dingtalkBound` 字段 |
| `src/mock/initialData.ts` | 初始 mock 数据，含 `dingtalkBound` |
| `src/features/mention/MentionPicker.tsx` | @提及选人组件，涉及 `dingtalkBound` 标识 |
| `src/features/task/NodeDetailDrawer.tsx` | 节点详情，涉及 `dingtalk` 日历展示 |

**规划文档**（`openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/`）：

| 文件 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| `proposal.md` | 变更提案：为什么做、做什么、影响范围 |
| `design.md` | 技术设计决策：fire-and-forget、token 缓存策略等 |
| `specs/dingtalk-service/spec.md` | `src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 的行为规范 |
| `specs/dingtalk-notification-dispatch/spec.md` | 通知调度集成规范 |
| `specs/user-management/spec.md` | 用户管理新增 `dingtalkUserId` 字段规范 |
| `specs/notification-center/spec.md` | `createNotification()` 集成规范 |
| `tasks.md` | 6 大类 17 个开发任务清单（全部待完成） |

---

### 总结

当前项目钉钉集成处于**"环境变量已配置、schema/接口/前端均尚未实现"**的状态：
- `.env` 中三个 `DINGTALK_*` 变量已有真实值
- `User` model 有 `dingtalkBound` 布尔字段，但缺少 `dingtalkUserId` 字段（计划新增）
- `src/lib/dingtalk.ts` 不存在（计划新建）
- 前端用户表单无 `dingtalkUserId` 输入框（计划新增）
- `openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/` 下已有完整的设计文档和任务清单，等待开发实施

**Title:** Analyze file lines and extract non-URL text

```json
{
  "command": "python3 -c \"\nwith open('/home/heyue/.local/share/opencode/tool-output/tool_e433c6c23001ehJKw57nID97at', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n    content = f.read()\n\n# 文件实际上只有3行，找出每行长度\nlines = content.split('\\n')\nprint(f'共 {len(lines)} 行')\nfor i, line in enumerate(lines):\n    print(f'第{i+1}行长度: {len(line)}')\n    if len(line) < 200:\n        print(f'内容: {repr(line)}')\n    else:\n        # 搜索这一行里的非URL内容\n        import re\n        text = re.sub(r'https?://[^\\s\\)\\]]+', '', line)\n        text = re.sub(r'[\\[\\]\\(\\)]+', ' ', text)\n        text = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', text).strip()\n        print(f'非URL内容（前2000字符）: {text[:2000]}')\n        print(f'非URL内容（后2000字符）: {text[-2000:]}')\n\"\n",

}
```

```
<content>
1: /**
2:  * 钉钉企业内部应用服务层
3:  *
4:  * 功能：
5:  *  1. access_token 获取与模块级缓存（过期前 5 分钟主动刷新）
6:  *  2. sendDingtalkWorkMessage — 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 类型）
7:  *  3. pushNotificationToDingtalk — 按数据库 recipientId 查 dingtalkUserId 后推送
8:  *
9:  * 设计决策（见 openspec/changes/dingtalk-notification/design.md）：
10:  *  - 推送失败只记录 logger.warn，不抛出异常（静默降级）
11:  *  - 环境变量缺失时直接跳过，不影响主业务
12:  *  - 使用旧版 API（oapi.dingtalk.com）发送工作通知，兼容性最好
13:  */
14: 
15: import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";
16: import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
17: 
18: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
19: // access_token 缓存
20: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
21: 
22: interface TokenCache {
23:   token: string;
24:   /** 过期时间戳（毫秒），到期前 5 分钟触发刷新 */
25:   expiresAt: number;
26: }
27: 
28: let tokenCache: TokenCache | null = null;
29: 
30: /**
31:  * 获取钉钉企业 access_token（含模块级缓存，过期前 5 分钟刷新）。
32:  * 环境变量 DINGTALK_APP_KEY / DINGTALK_APP_SECRET 缺失时返回 null。
33:  */
34: async function getDingtalkToken(): Promise<string | null> {
35:   const appKey = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_KEY;
36:   const appSecret = process.env.DINGTALK_APP_SECRET;
37: 
38:   if (!appKey || !appSecret) {
39:     return null;
40:   }
41: 
42:   const now = Date.now();
43:   // 提前 5 分钟（300_000 ms）刷新，避免临界过期
44:   if (tokenCache && tokenCache.expiresAt - 300_000 > now) {
45:     return tokenCache.token;
46:   }
47: 
48:   try {
49:     const url = `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/gettoken?appkey=${encodeURIComponent(appKey)}&appsecret=${encodeURIComponent(appSecret)}`;
50:     const res = await fetch(url, { method: "GET" });
51:     const data = (await res.json()) as {
52:       errcode: number;
53:       errmsg: string;
54:       access_token?: string;
55:       expires_in?: number;
56:     };
57: 
58:     if (data.errcode !== 0 || !data.access_token) {
59:       logger.warn(
60:         { service: "dingtalk" },
61:         `获取钉钉 access_token 失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,
62:       );
63:       return null;
64:     }
65: 
66:     // expires_in 单位为秒，默认 7200
67:     const expiresIn = (data.expires_in ?? 7200) * 1000;
68:     tokenCache = {
69:       token: data.access_token,
70:       expiresAt: now + expiresIn,
71:     };
72:     return tokenCache.token;
73:   } catch (err) {
74:     logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk", err }, "请求钉钉 access_token 异常");
75:     return null;
76:   }
77: }
78: 
79: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
80: // 发送工作通知
81: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
82: 
83: /**
84:  * 向指定钉钉用户发送工作通知（text 纯文本类型）。
85:  *
86:  * @param dingtalkUserId 钉钉用户 userId 或 unionId（由管理员录入）
87:  * @param content        消息正文（建议格式：`【工作平台】${title}\n${body}`）
88:  *
89:  * 失败时仅 logger.warn，不抛出异常。
90:  */
91: export async function sendDingtalkWorkMessage(
92:   dingtalkUserId: string,
93:   content: string,
94: ): Promise<void> {
95:   const agentIdStr = process.env.DINGTALK_AGENT_ID;
96:   if (!agentIdStr) {
97:     logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk" }, "DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 未配置，跳过推送");
98:     return;
99:   }
100: 
101:   const agentId = parseInt(agentIdStr, 10);
102:   if (isNaN(agentId)) {
103:     logger.warn(
104:       { service: "dingtalk" },
105:       `DINGTALK_AGENT_ID 格式无效（非整数）：${agentIdStr}`,
106:     );
107:     return;
108:   }
109: 
110:   const token = await getDingtalkToken();
111:   if (!token) {
112:     // getDingtalkToken 内部已记录 warn，此处不重复
113:     return;
114:   }
115: 
116:   try {
117:     const res = await fetch(
118:       `https://oapi.dingtalk.com/topapi/message/corpconversation/asyncsend_v2?access_token=${token}`,
119:       {
120:         method: "POST",
121:         headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
122:         body: JSON.stringify({
123:           agent_id: agentId,
124:           userid_list: dingtalkUserId,
125:           msg: {
126:             msgtype: "text",
127:             text: { content },
128:           },
129:         }),
130:       },
131:     );
132: 
133:     const data = (await res.json()) as {
134:       errcode: number;
135:       errmsg: string;
136:     };
137: 
138:     if (data.errcode !== 0) {
139:       logger.warn(
140:         { service: "dingtalk", dingtalkUserId },
141:         `钉钉工作通知发送失败：errcode=${data.errcode} errmsg=${data.errmsg}`,
142:       );
143:     }
144:   } catch (err) {
145:     logger.warn(
146:       { service: "dingtalk", dingtalkUserId, err },
147:       "发送钉钉工作通知异常",
148:     );
149:   }
150: }
151: 
152: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
153: // 按 recipientId 推送通知（供 workspace route 调用）
154: // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
155: 
156: export interface PendingDingtalkNotif {
157:   recipientId: number;
158:   title: string;
159:   body?: string | null;
160: }
161: 
162: /**
163:  * 批量推送待发钉钉通知（fire-and-forget 场景）。
164:  *
165:  * 对每条通知：
166:  *  1. 查询接收者的 dingtalkUserId
167:  *  2. 若非空，调用 sendDingtalkWorkMessage
168:  *
169:  * 整个函数不抛出异常，失败均 logger.warn 静默处理。
170:  */
171: export async function pushPendingDingtalkNotifs(
172:   notifs: PendingDingtalkNotif[],
173: ): Promise<void> {
174:   if (notifs.length === 0) return;
175: 
176:   // 去重 recipientId，批量查询
177:   const recipientIds = [...new Set(notifs.map((n) => n.recipientId))];
178: 
179:   let userMap: Map<number, string>;
180:   try {
181:     const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
182:       where: {
183:         id: { in: recipientIds },
184:         dingtalkUserId: { not: null },
185:       },
186:       select: { id: true, dingtalkUserId: true },
187:     });
188:     userMap = new Map(
189:       users
190:         .filter((u) => u.dingtalkUserId)
191:         .map((u) => [u.id, u.dingtalkUserId!]),
192:     );
193:   } catch (err) {
194:     logger.warn({ service: "dingtalk", err }, "查询用户 dingtalkUserId 异常，跳过推送");
195:     return;
196:   }
197: 
198:   // 逐条推送（不并发，避免触发钉钉限流）
199:   for (const notif of notifs) {
200:     const dingtalkUserId = userMap.get(notif.recipientId);
201:     if (!dingtalkUserId) continue;
202: 
203:     const content = notif.body
204:       ? `【工作平台】${notif.title}\n${notif.body}`
205:       : `【工作平台】${notif.title}`;
206: 
207:     // fire-and-forget：不 await，不阻塞调用方
208:     void sendDingtalkWorkMessage(dingtalkUserId, content);
209:   }
210: }

(End of file - total 210 lines)
```

```
15: // ── PATCH ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
16: async function patchHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
17:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
18: 
19:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
20:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
21:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
22:   }
23: 
24:   const targetId = parseInt((ctx?.params as Record<string, string>)?.id ?? "");
25:   if (isNaN(targetId)) {
26:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
27:   }
28: 
29:   const target = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: targetId } });
30:   if (!target) {
31:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 });
32:   }
33: 
34:   const body = (await req.json()) as {
35:     name?: string;
36:     email?: string;
37:     avatar?: string;
38:     departmentId?: string;
39:     jobTitle?: string;
40:     status?: string;
41:     isAdmin?: boolean;
42:     managerId?: string | null;
43:     dingtalkUserId?: string | null;
44:   };
45: 
46:   // 部门存在性校验
47:   if (body.departmentId !== undefined) {
48:     const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(body.departmentId) } });
49:     if (!dept) {
50:       return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
51:     }
52:   }
53: 
54:   // 直接上级存在性校验
55:   let managerDbId: number | null | undefined = undefined;
56:   if (body.managerId !== undefined) {
57:     if (body.managerId === null || body.managerId === "") {
58:       managerDbId = null;
59:     } else {
60:       const mid = parseInt(body.managerId);
61:       if (isNaN(mid)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
62:       if (mid === targetId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能将自己设为自己的上级" }, { status: 400 });
63:       const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: mid } });
64:       if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
65:       managerDbId = mid;
66:     }
67:   }
68: 
69:   // 禁止把自己的 isAdmin 去掉（防止锁死系统）
70:   if (targetId === userId && body.isAdmin === false) {
71:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "不能取消自己的管理员权限" }, { status: 400 });
72:   }
73: 
74:   const updated = await prisma.user.update({
75:     where: { id: targetId },
76:     data: {
77:       ...(body.name !== undefined && { name: body.name.trim() }),
78:       ...(body.email !== undefined && { email: body.email.trim() }),
79:       ...(body.avatar !== undefined && { avatar: body.avatar.trim() || null }),
80:       ...(body.departmentId !== undefined && { departmentId: parseInt(body.departmentId) }),
81:       ...(body.jobTitle !== undefined && { jobTitle: body.jobTitle.trim() }),
82:       ...(body.status !== undefined && { status: body.status }),
83:       ...(body.isAdmin !== undefined && { isAdmin: body.isAdmin }),
84:       ...(managerDbId !== undefined && { managerId: managerDbId }),
85:       // dingtalkUserId：非空字符串→写入并置 dingtalkBound=true；空/null→清空并置 dingtalkBound=false
86:       ...(body.dingtalkUserId !== undefined && {
87:         dingtalkUserId: body.dingtalkUserId?.trim() || null,
88:         dingtalkBound: !!(body.dingtalkUserId?.trim()),
89:       }),
90:     },
91:     select: {
92:       id: true,
93:       employeeNo: true,
94:       name: true,
95:       email: true,
96:       avatar: true,
97:       departmentId: true,
98:       jobTitle: true,
99:       status: true,
100:       isAdmin: true,
101:       dingtalkBound: true,
102:       dingtalkUserId: true,
103:       managerId: true,
104:       mustResetPassword: true,
105:     },
106:   });
107: 
108:   // 同步 OrgRelation：managerId 字段有变更时，重建实线汇报关系
109:   if (managerDbId !== undefined) {
110:     // 删除该用户现有的所有实线上级关系
111:     await prisma.orgRelation.deleteMany({
112:       where: { subordinateId: targetId, relationType: "solid" },
113:     });
114:     if (managerDbId !== null) {
115:       const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
116:       await prisma.orgRelation.create({
117:         data: {
118:           subordinateId: targetId,
119:           managerId: managerDbId,
120:           relationType: "solid",
121:           effectiveFrom: today,
122:           effectiveTo: null,
123:         },
124:       });
125:       logger.info(
126:         { user: userId },
127:         `同步 OrgRelation：用户 ${targetId} → 新上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
128:       );
129:     } else {
130:       logger.info(
131:         { user: userId },
132:         `同步 OrgRelation：清除用户 ${targetId} 的实线上级关系`,
133:       );
134:     }
135:   }
136: 
137:   logger.info({ user: userId }, `管理员更新用户 ${targetId}：${JSON.stringify(body)}`);
138: 
139:   return NextResponse.json({
140:     user: {
141:       id: String(updated.id),
142:       employeeNo: updated.employeeNo,
143:       name: updated.name,
144:       email: updated.email,
145:       avatar: updated.avatar ?? undefined,
146:       departmentId: String(updated.departmentId),
147:       jobTitle: updated.jobTitle,
148:       status: updated.status,

154:     },

159: async function deleteHandler(req: NextRequest, ctx?: { params?: Record<string, string> }): Promise<NextResponse> {
160:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
161: 
162:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
163:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {

186:   });
187:

189: 
190:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true });
```

```
42: function authHeaders() {
43:   return { "Content-Type": "application/json", Authorization: `Bearer ${getApiToken()}` };
44: }
45: 
46: export default function AdminUsersPage() {
47:   const router = useRouter();
48:   const { currentUser, refreshWorkspace } = useStore();
49: 
50:   const [users, setUsers] = useState<AdminUser[]>([]);
51:   const [depts, setDepts] = useState<Dept[]>([]);
52:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
53: 
54:   // 新建/编辑对话框
55:   const [showForm, setShowForm] = useState(false);
56:   const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);
57:   const [form, setForm] = useState({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "", dingtalkUserId: "" });
58:   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
59: 
60:   // 禁用确认
61:   const [disableTarget, setDisableTarget] = useState<AdminUser | null>(null);
62: 
63:   // 权限检查
64:   useEffect(() => {
65:     if (currentUser && !currentUser.isAdmin) {
66:       router.replace("/mindmap");
67:     }
68:   }, [currentUser, router]);
69: 
70:   const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
71:     setLoading(true);
72:     try {
73:       const [uRes, dRes] = await Promise.all([
74:         fetch("/api/admin/users", { headers: authHeaders() }),
75:         fetch("/api/admin/departments", { headers: authHeaders() }),
76:       ]);
77:       const uJson = await uRes.json() as { users?: AdminUser[]; error?: string };
78:       const dJson = await dRes.json() as { departments?: Dept[]; error?: string };
79:       if (!uRes.ok) throw new Error(uJson.error ?? "加载用户失败");
80:       if (!dRes.ok) throw new Error(dJson.error ?? "加载部门失败");
81:       setUsers(uJson.users ?? []);
82:       setDepts(dJson.departments ?? []);
83:     } catch (e) {
84:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
85:     } finally {
86:       setLoading(false);
87:     }
88:   }, []);
89: 
90:   useEffect(() => { void fetchData(); }, [fetchData]);
91: 
92:   function openCreate() {
93:     setEditTarget(null);
94:     setForm({ employeeNo: "", name: "", email: "", avatar: "", departmentId: depts[0]?.id ?? "", jobTitle: "", managerId: "", dingtalkUserId: "" });
95:     setShowForm(true);
96:   }
97: 
98:   function openEdit(u: AdminUser) {
99:     setEditTarget(u);
100:     setForm({ employeeNo: u.employeeNo, name: u.name, email: u.email, avatar: u.avatar ?? "", departmentId: u.departmentId, jobTitle: u.jobTitle, managerId: u.managerId ?? "", dingtalkUserId: u.dingtalkUserId ?? "" });
101:     setShowForm(true);
102:   }
103: 
104:   async function handleSave() {
105:     if (!form.name.trim()) { toast.error("姓名不能为空"); return; }
106:     if (!form.departmentId) { toast.error("请选择部门"); return; }
107:     if (!form.jobTitle.trim()) { toast.error("职位不能为空"); return; }
108:     if (!editTarget && !form.employeeNo.trim()) { toast.error("工号不能为空"); return; }
109: 
110:     setSaving(true);
111:     try {
112:       if (editTarget) {
113:         const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${editTarget.id}`, {
114:           method: "PATCH",
115:           headers: authHeaders(),
116:           body: JSON.stringify({
117:             name: form.name,
118:             email: form.email,
119:             avatar: form.avatar,
120:             departmentId: form.departmentId,
121:             jobTitle: form.jobTitle,
122:             managerId: form.managerId || null,
123:             dingtalkUserId: form.dingtalkUserId.trim() || null,
124:           }),
125:         });
126:         const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
127:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "更新失败");
128:         setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === editTarget.id ? (d.user ?? u) : u));
129:         toast.success("用户信息已更新");
130:         // PATCH 总是包含 managerId，可能改变 OrgRelation，刷新全局 relations
131:         void refreshWorkspace();
132:       } else {
133:         const r = await fetch("/api/admin/users", {
134:           method: "POST",
135:           headers: authHeaders(),
136:           body: JSON.stringify({ ...form, managerId: form.managerId || undefined }),
137:         });
138:         const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
139:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "创建失败");
140:         setUsers(prev => [...prev, d.user!]);
141:         toast.success(`用户 ${form.name} 创建成功，初始密码：123456`);
142:         // 新用户若有直属上级，刷新全局 relations
143:         if (form.managerId) void refreshWorkspace();
144:       }
145:       setShowForm(false);
146:     } catch (e) {
147:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
148:     } finally {
149:       setSaving(false);
150:     }
151:   }
152: 
153:   async function handleDisable() {
154:     if (!disableTarget) return;
155:     try {
156:       const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${disableTarget.id}`, {
157:         method: "DELETE",
158:         headers: authHeaders(),
159:       });
160:       const d = await r.json() as { ok?: boolean; error?: string };
161:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
162:       setUsers(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === disableTarget.id ? { ...u, status: "disabled" } : u));
163:       toast.success(`用户 ${disableTarget.name} 已禁用`);
164:     } catch (e) {
165:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
166:     } finally {
167:       setDisableTarget(null);
168:     }
169:   }
170: 
171:   async function handleEnable(u: AdminUser) {
172:     try {
173:       const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}`, {
174:         method: "PATCH",
175:         headers: authHeaders(),
176:         body: JSON.stringify({ status: "active" }),
177:       });
178:       const d = await r.json() as { user?: AdminUser; error?: string };
179:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(d.error ?? "操作失败");
180:       setUsers(prev => prev.map(usr => usr.id === u.id ? { ...usr, status: "active" } : usr));
181:       toast.success(`用户 ${u.name} 已启用`);
182:     } catch (e) {
183:       toast.error((e as Error).message);
184:     }
185:   }
186: 
187:   function deptName(id: string) {
188:     return depts.find(d => d.id === id)?.name ?? id;
189:   }
190: 
191:   return (
192:     <>
193:       <PageHeader
194:         title="用户管理"
195:         description="管理系统用户账号，新建用户初始密码为 123456"
196:         right={
197:           <Button onClick={openCreate} size="sm">
198:             <UserPlus className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
199:             新建用户
200:           </Button>
201:         }
202:       />
203: 
204:       <div className="flex-1 p-6 overflow-auto">
205:         {loading ? (
206:           <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">加载中…</div>
207:         ) : (
208:           <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border border-border overflow-hidden">
209:             <table className="w-full text-sm">
210:               <thead className="bg-slate-50 border-b border-border">
211:                 <tr>
212:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">工号</th>
213:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">姓名</th>
214:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">部门</th>
215:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">职位</th>
216:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">状态</th>
217:                   <th className="text-left px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">角色</th>
218:                   <th className="text-right px-4 py-3 text-muted-foreground font-medium">操作</th>
219:                 </tr>
220:               </thead>
221:               <tbody className="divide-y divide-border">
222:                 {users.map(u => (
223:                   <tr key={u.id} className="hover:bg-slate-50">
224:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{u.employeeNo}</td>
225:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 font-medium text-brand-ink">
226:                       {u.avatar ? <span className="mr-1">{u.avatar}</span> : null}
227:                       {u.name}
228:                     </td>
229:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{deptName(u.departmentId)}</td>
230:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">{u.jobTitle}</td>
231:                     <td className="px-4 py-3">
232:                       <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${u.status === "active" ? "bg-green-50 text-green-700" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-500"}`}>
233:                         {u.status === "active" ? "正常" : "已禁用"}
234:                       </span>
235:                     </td>
236:                     <td className="px-4 py-3">
237:                       {u.isAdmin && (
238:                         <span className="inline-flex px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-orange-50 text-orange-700">管理员</span>
239:                       )}
240:                     </td>
241:                     <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
242:                       <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">
243:                         <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => openEdit(u)} title="编辑">
244:                           <Pencil className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
245:                         </Button>
246:                         {u.status === "active" ? (
247:                           <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => setDisableTarget(u)} title="禁用" disabled={u.id === currentUser?.id}>
248:                             <Ban className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-destructive" />
249:                           </Button>
250:                         ) : (
251:                           <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => handleEnable(u)} title="启用">
252:                             <CheckCircle2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-600" />
253:                           </Button>
254:                         )}
255:                       </div>
256:                     </td>
257:                   </tr>
258:                 ))}
259:                 {users.length === 0 && (
260:                   <tr>
261:                     <td colSpan={7} className="px-4 py-10 text-center text-muted-foreground">
262:                       暂无用户，请点击右上角新建
263:                     </td>
264:                   </tr>
265:                 )}
266:               </tbody>
267:             </table>
268:           </div>
269:         )}
270:       </div>
271: 
272:       {/* 新建/编辑对话框 */}
273:       <Dialog open={showForm} onOpenChange={setShowForm}>
274:         <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
275:           <DialogHeader>
276:             <DialogTitle>{editTarget ? "编辑用户" : "新建用户"}</DialogTitle>
277:           </DialogHeader>
278:           <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
279:             {!editTarget && (
280:               <div className="space-y-1.5">
281:                 <Label>工号 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
282:                 <Input value={form.employeeNo} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, employeeNo: e.target.value }))} placeholder="如 E011" />
283:               </div>
284:             )}
285:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
286:               <Label>姓名 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
287:               <Input value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, name: e.target.value }))} placeholder="真实姓名" />
288:             </div>
289:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
290:               <Label>邮箱</Label>

294:               <Label>头像（emoji）</Label>

300:                 className="w-full border border-input rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm bg-background"

302:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, departmentId: e.target.value }))}
303:               >

313:             </div>

324:                   .map(u => (
```

```
<content>
1: /**
2:  * GET  /api/admin/users  — 查询用户列表（仅管理员）
3:  * POST /api/admin/users  — 创建用户，初始密码固定为 123456（仅管理员）
4:  *
5:  * 规范 1-4：withApiLogger 包裹
6:  * 规范 4-2：操作前校验 isAdmin
7:  * 规范 4-3：getAuth 鉴权
8:  */
9: 
10: import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
11: import { withApiLogger } from "@/lib/withApiLogger";
12: import { prisma } from "@/lib/prisma";
13: import { getAuth } from "@/lib/auth";
14: import { hashPassword } from "@/lib/auth";
15: import { logger } from "@/lib/logger";
16: 
17: /** 初始密码（管理员创建用户时使用，用户首次登录后应自行修改） */
18: const INITIAL_PASSWORD = "123456";
19: 
20: // ── 工具：序列化用户行 ──────────────────────────────────────────
21: function serializeUser(u: {
22:   id: number;
23:   employeeNo: string;
24:   name: string;
25:   email: string;
26:   avatar: string | null;
27:   departmentId: number;
28:   jobTitle: string;
29:   status: string;
30:   isAdmin: boolean;
31:   dingtalkBound: boolean;
32:   dingtalkUserId: string | null;
33:   managerId: number | null;
34:   mustResetPassword: boolean;
35: }) {
36:   return {
37:     id: String(u.id),
38:     employeeNo: u.employeeNo,
39:     name: u.name,
40:     email: u.email,
41:     avatar: u.avatar ?? undefined,
42:     departmentId: String(u.departmentId),
43:     jobTitle: u.jobTitle,
44:     status: u.status,
45:     isAdmin: u.isAdmin,
46:     dingtalkBound: u.dingtalkBound,
47:     dingtalkUserId: u.dingtalkUserId ?? undefined,
48:     managerId: u.managerId ? String(u.managerId) : undefined,
49:     mustResetPassword: u.mustResetPassword,
50:   };
51: }
52: 
53: // ── GET ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
54: async function getHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
55:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
56: 
57:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
58:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
59:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可访问" }, { status: 403 });
60:   }
61: 
62:   const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
63:     orderBy: { id: "asc" },
64:     select: {
65:       id: true,
66:       employeeNo: true,
67:       name: true,
68:       email: true,
69:       avatar: true,
70:       departmentId: true,
71:       jobTitle: true,
72:       status: true,
73:       isAdmin: true,
74:       dingtalkBound: true,
75:       dingtalkUserId: true,
76:       managerId: true,
77:       mustResetPassword: true,
78:     },
79:   });
80: 
81:   return NextResponse.json({ users: users.map(serializeUser) });
82: }
83: 
84: // ── POST ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
85: async function postHandler(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
86:   const { userId } = await getAuth(req);
87: 
88:   const me = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
89:   if (!me?.isAdmin) {
90:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "无权限，仅管理员可操作" }, { status: 403 });
91:   }
92: 
93:   const body = (await req.json()) as {
94:     employeeNo?: string;
95:     name?: string;
96:     email?: string;
97:     departmentId?: string;
98:     jobTitle?: string;
99:     avatar?: string;
100:     managerId?: string;
101:   };
102: 
103:   const { employeeNo, name, email, departmentId, jobTitle, avatar, managerId } = body;
104: 
105:   if (!employeeNo?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
106:   if (!name?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "姓名不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
107:   if (!departmentId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
108:   if (!jobTitle?.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: "职位不能为空" }, { status: 400 });
109: 
110:   // 工号唯一性校验
111:   const existing = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { employeeNo: employeeNo.trim() } });
112:   if (existing) {
113:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "工号已存在" }, { status: 409 });
114:   }
115: 
116:   // 部门存在性校验（规范 4-2：后端独立鉴权，不信任前端传值）
117:   const dept = await prisma.department.findUnique({ where: { id: parseInt(departmentId) } });
118:   if (!dept) {
119:     return NextResponse.json({ error: "部门不存在" }, { status: 400 });
120:   }
121: 
122:   // 直接上级存在性校验（如果指定）
123:   let managerDbId: number | null = null;
124:   if (managerId) {
125:     managerDbId = parseInt(managerId);
126:     if (isNaN(managerDbId)) return NextResponse.json({ error: "直接上级 ID 无效" }, { status: 400 });
127:     const mgr = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: managerDbId } });
128:     if (!mgr) return NextResponse.json({ error: "指定的直接上级不存在" }, { status: 400 });
129:   }
130: 
131:   const passwordHash = await hashPassword(INITIAL_PASSWORD);
132: 
133:   const created = await prisma.user.create({
134:     data: {
135:       employeeNo: employeeNo.trim(),
136:       name: name.trim(),
137:       email: email?.trim() || `${employeeNo.trim()}@company.local`,
138:       avatar: avatar?.trim() || null,
139:       departmentId: parseInt(departmentId),
140:       jobTitle: jobTitle.trim(),
141:       status: "active",
142:       passwordHash,
143:       isAdmin: false,
144:       managerId: managerDbId,
145:       mustResetPassword: true,
146:     },
147:     select: {
148:       id: true,
149:       employeeNo: true,
150:       name: true,
151:       email: true,
152:       avatar: true,
153:       departmentId: true,
154:       jobTitle: true,
155:       status: true,
156:       isAdmin: true,
157:       dingtalkBound: true,
158:       dingtalkUserId: true,
159:       managerId: true,
160:       mustResetPassword: true,
161:     },
162:   });
163: 
164:   // 同步 OrgRelation：若设置了直属上级，创建实线汇报关系
165:   if (managerDbId) {
166:     const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
167:     await prisma.orgRelation.create({
168:       data: {
169:         subordinateId: created.id,
170:         managerId: managerDbId,
171:         relationType: "solid",
172:         effectiveFrom: today,
173:         effectiveTo: null,
174:       },
175:     });
176:     logger.info(
177:       { user: userId },
178:       `同步 OrgRelation：新用户 ${created.id} → 上级 ${managerDbId}（solid）`,
179:     );
180:   }
181: 
182:   logger.info(
183:     { user: userId },
184:     `管理员创建用户：${created.employeeNo} ${created.name}`,
185:   );
186: 
187:   return NextResponse.json({ user: serializeUser(created) }, { status: 201 });
188: }
189: 
190: export const GET = withApiLogger(getHandler);
191: export const POST = withApiLogger(postHandler);

(End of file - total 191 lines)
</content>
```
